¶the actis deidis illuſter vailȝeand campioun schir william wallace knicht ellerſlie ☞ ✚ ☜ ¶ ¶the firſt buik ovr anteceſſouris ſuld reid hald mynd yair nobill douchtie deid let ouir ſlyde throw verray ſleuthfulnes caſtis v euer vther beſynes vane gamming ſet haill intent quhilk he bene ſene till thir tymis went nixt nichtbouris cūmin brutus blude oftentymis scottis willit lytill gude thocht lait god turnit yair mynd greit kyndnes yai haue ſchawin v till hartis pepill lord he hand may yame reu • gyde command thocht leidis wald haue yi lād thrall oppone power god aganis thame haue ſene foirbearis afoir bot thir parabillis ſpeik moir ¶we reid ane richt famous renoun worthy blude regnit regioun hyne furth purpois hald william wallace ȝe haue hard heir tald foirbearis quha lykis vnderſtand auld lynnage trew blude scotland schir rannald craufurd richt schiref air swa tyme ane docher fair ȝoung schir rannald schiref yat toun siſter fair gude fame renoun malcolme wallace hir gat mariage ellerſlie heritage auchin bothy mony ane vther place ſecund oye gude wallace quhilk wallace full hardely wrocht quhen walter heir wallace ſocht quha lykis heir mair knawledge yat part ga reid lyne firſt stewart bot malcolme wallace gat lady bricht malcolme wallace ane full gude gentill knicht william al cronicklis beiris hand quhilk efter reſkewer scotland quhen loiſt treſſoun falſnes ouir ſet fais fred throw goddis grace king alexander worthy king forlorne auenture lyfe kingorne thre ȝeiris ſtill ye realme ſtude deſolait quhair throw yair rais ane full greuous debait prince dauid erll huntingtoun thre dochteris gude fame renoun ye quhilk thre come bruce balliol haiſting twa thir thre deſyrit king ballioll clamit ye firſt gre lynely bruce firſt maill ye ſecund gre edward ſone vnto ingland thay ſend greit ſtryfe thocht yai ſuld mak ane end foly forſuith hapnit ſa succour ſeik thair auld mortall fa edward langſchankis new begun weir vpon gaſcone ane awfull feir thay landis quhilkis clamit ſtude ſic cais thocht fra hand mak haill conqueis norhame kirk come withouttin mair counſall yan scotland met thair full ſubtellie chargit thame bandoun thair ouirlord hald crown biſchop robert tyme full worthy glaſgow lord ſaid deny ony ouirlord bot greit god abuif king wraith hame remuif ȝit iohne ballioll followit ſa faſt hald grantit laſt contrair richt ane king maid yair quhair throw scotland repentit full ſair ballioll lordis wald nocht conſent edward furth ſet doun ane parliament callit ballioll anſwer scotland wyſe lordis gart ſone brek yat band ane abbot paſt gaif ouir alledgeance king edward yan tuik greit greuance oiſt raiſit come werk tweid bot fecht yan greit dreid corſpatrik dunbar ſone ſend counſall aſkit countrie kend fra brocht preſence king ſubtell band yai cordit thing ¶the wynning berwik cap ij erll patrik berwik couth perſew reſſauit traiſtit verray trew king followit men renoun • ter mydnicht reſt toun corſpatrik rais keyis weill knew leit briggis doun portcuilleis thay knew edward enterit gart ſla haiſtely men wyfis aucht thouſand fyfty barnis al fals auenture trew scottis chaipit na creature ane capitane thair fals king he maid towart dunbar without reſting thay raid ¶the battell dunbar cap iij qvhair gadderit greit power ſcotlād aganis edward battell ſtand thir four erllis enterit place mat menteith athoill vpon cace caſtell erll gart hald thame thair men without yai micht win ȝit thame ſuppleing battellis togidder faſt thay ga full greit ſlauchter yat pietie ſe trew scottis ouir ſet ſubteltie erll patrik quhen fechting fellaiſt fa turnit harming v maiſt nane warld yat ſkaithis may mair weill traiſtit borne familiar men ar ſlane without redemptioun throw thir deidis haill tynt regioun ¶how king edward corſpatrik come • one put doun iohne ballioun yame ye • ri scotland cap iiij ☞ ✚ ☜ king edward paſt corſpatrik scone thair gat homage scotland ſone nane left ye realme defend iohne ballioll yan montros yat ſend depryuit ay kingrik edward ſelf callit ane royall rik crown tuik vpon ye ſamin ſtane gathelus ſend sone fra spayne quhen yber scot firſt scotland came canmore ſyne king fergus name brocht scone gart ſtabill thair quhair kingis war crownit viij hūdreth ȝeir mair befoir tyme yat king edward fand thir iowellis gart turs ingland londoun ſet witnes thing conqueis yan scotland maid king quhair yt ſtane ſtandis scotlād ſuld maiſter god cheis ye tyme margaretis airis ſe aucht ſcoir thay led greiteſt yat yai fand airis thame bruce scotland office bruikit bot ſchort tyme may put ye deidis ryme cronicklis quhy ſuld tary lang wallace agane breifly gang scotland loiſt quhen bot ane chyld haill ouir ſet enemeis wyld father malcolme lennox fled eldeſt sone thidder led mother fled fra ellerſlie gowrie paſt dwelt kilſpindie knicht hir father thidder thame ſent vnto vncle ane gude intent gowrie dwelt thair leuing thair ane agit man quhilk reſſauit thame fair dundie wallace scuill thay ſend quhill wit full worthely kend thus continewit tender age armis ſyne mony vaſſallage quhen saroun blude regioū couth ring markand vnrichteous king mony greit wrang yai wrocht regioun deſtroyit lordis brak yair biggingis doun baith wyfis wedowis yai tuik yair awin nūnis madynnis quhom yai lykit ſpil king herodis part yai playit scotland ȝoung chyldren yat yai befoir yame fand biſchoprikis greiteſt vaill thay tuik handis yair archebiſchoppis haill nocht pape yai wald na kirkis forbeir bot grippit violence weir glaſgow yai gaif thair waill kend diocie durhame ane commend small benefice yan yai wald nocht perſew bot thing full mony vther yai ſlew hangit barrounis wrocht full mekill cair weill knawin within barnis air thair auchtene ſcoir put ane felloun dreid bot god abuif he ſend v ſum remeid rememberit farther taill follow vpon purpois haill william wallace man armis greit pietie thocht yat scotland tuik ſic harmis mekill dolour mynd wyſe richt worthy wicht kynd gowrie dwelt ſtill yi worthy man increſſit abandoun hart full mekill cair ſaw sutheroun multiplie mair mair ſelf oft wald mak mane gude kyn yai ſlane mony ane ȝit ſemely ſtark bald age ſeuintene wynter ald wappinnis bair outher gude ſword knyife thame hapnit richt oft ſtryife quhair fand ane ane vtheris preſence▪ efter scottis thay na mair offence cut throit ſtik ſuddandly waynit nocht fand yame anerly sindrie wantit bot nane wiſt quhat way yair couth na man ocht ſay lytill ſpeiche courtes bening sad countenance baith ald ȝing ¶how wallace ſlew ȝoung selbie conſtabillis sone dundie cap v vpone ane day dundie ſend cruelnes full lytill thay kend cōſtabill ane felloun man weir vntill scottis full mekill deir selbie hecht dſpiteous outrage ane sone neir twentie ȝeir age tſhe toun vſit euerie day thre men four yairto play ane hielie ſchrew wantoun intent wallace ſaw towart went lyklie richt big weill beſene intill ane weid gudly ganand grene callit ſaid thow scot abyde quha deuil quod graithit ſa guid weid ane hors mantill war thy kynd weir ane scottis quhittill vnder thy belt beir rouch rillingis vpon thy harlotis feit gif thy knyfe quhat doi thy geir ſa meit ȝeid knyfe tak fra faſt collar wallace ta vnder hand knyfe braidit men yat ſemblit bot help ſelf wiſt na remeid without reſkew ſtikkit deid squyar fell yair na mair men followit wallace wounder ſair preis thick cūmerit yame full faſt wallace ſpedy greitly al agaſt bludy knyfe drawin hand ſpairit nane befoir fand hous knew eme ludgit thidder fled farther micht nocht win gude wyfe thair within clois ſaw help cryit yat deit tre ȝoung capitane he fallin ſtryfe dur went gude wyfe ane ruſſat gown hir awin ſcho gaif abone weid couerit laif ane ſuddillit courche ouir nek heid leit fall ane worne quhyte hat ſcho braiſſit yai ſuld nocht lang tary gaif ane rock ſyne ſat doun ſpin sutheroun ſocht quhair wallace dreid thay wiſt weill quhat ȝet ȝeid ſame hous thay ſocht beſely bot ſat ſtill ſpan richt cūnandly tyme nocht leirit lang thay left ſa furth gait gang heuy cheir ſorrowfull thocht na wit yan get culd thay nocht ingliſmen barrat boun bad fyre scottis war toun ȝit gude wyfe held wallace vntill nicht maid gude cheir ſyne put ſicht throw ane dirk gait ſcho gydit full faſt couert went ſyne vp watter paſt forbure gait wachis thair mother ane greit deſpair quhen ſcho ſaw ſcho thankit heuinis king ſaid deir sone ſa lang quhair he yow bene tauld mother ſuddand cace weipit ſcho ſaid full oft allace thow ceis thow ſlane mother ſaid god reuilar vnſufferabill pepill ingland part thair ire think ſuld ganeſtand eme wiſt weill squyar ſlew dreid thairof greit langour drew paſſit ouir quhill diuers dayis war gane gude man dred wallace ſuld tane sutheroun ar full ſubtell euerilk man ane greit dittay scottis ordanit yai yan law dayis dundie ſet ane air wallace wald na langer soiorne thair mother graithit hir ane pilgrame weid ſelf diſagyſit ſyne glaidly hir ȝeid ane ſchort ſword vnder weid bair land full mony fais baith yair fuit yame mair tuik yai nocht quha ſpeirit ſcho ſaid sanct margaret thay ſocht quha ſeruit hir ful greit freindſchip yai fād sutheroun folk ſcho ingland beſyde lundoris ferry ouir thay paſt syne throw ochell ſped yai wounder faſt dunfermeling thay ludgit nicht vpon ye morne quhen day lichr gentill wemen hapnit thame pa ingland borne lynlithgow wynnād capitanis wyfe pilgramage bene fra ſcho thame met ȝoung wallace ſene gude cheir thay maid wounder fair nocht large toung weill taucht debonair furth talk thus materis yat war wrocht quhill ſouth ouir forth hir sone ſcho yame brocht lynlithgow yai wald tary lang thair leif thay tuik donypace thay gang thair dwelt eme ane man greit rich michtie perſoun hecht name wallace maid yame gude cheir ane full gude man welcūmit yame fair thame tald wit land ſteir tretit thame weill ſaid sone ſa deir thy mother yow richt heir ſall byde quhill better chance may betyde wallace anſwerit ſaid weſtir mair kyn ſlane lykis euill vther mony worthy art leif god ſall v wreik part perſoun ſichit ſaid sone ſa fre nocht wit redres may quhat ſuld ſpeik fruſtrair tyde gift gude wald nocht byde mother ellerſlie thay went vpon morne ſcho hir brether ſent corſbie dwelt schiref air father deid leuit lang tyme thair hir eldeſt sone yat mekill mane hir huſband al lochmabane ſlane schir malcolme wallace name lei hoch ſennounis cuttit preis kneis faucht feill ingliſmen thay ſlew ſocht fechtaris anew ather ſyde ſpeiris bair doun thair ſtickit thay yat gude knicht renoun vnto taill left ellerſly schir rannald come vnto siſter fre welcūmit thame hame ſpeirit yair intent scho prayit lord peirſe wald went scho irkit weir ſcho culd na farther fle purches peice reſt ſcho micht schir rannald peirſeis protectioun part tak remiſſioun gart wryte siſter tyde reſpect wallace wald nocht abyde mother left ſcho weipit hart full ſair leif tuik ſyne fra eme fair ȝoung sutheroun richt ſauage greit rowme yai deſpyte eik outrage schir rannald durſt weill wallace yair greit perrell wiſt appeirand wair yai haill ſtrenthis land quhat yai wald durſt nane aganis yame ſtād schiref vſit thame amang full ſair dred yat wallace ſuld tak wrang thay culd neuer weill accord gat ane blaw thocht lad lord profferit ony lichtlynes bot thay repairit ouir mekill place al inglis clerkis prophecie fand ane wallace ſuld put yame fra scotland schir rannald knew weill ane mair quyet ſteid quhair william micht better fra thair feid vncle wallace ricardtoun schir richard hecht gude knicht renoū thay landis haill heritage bot blynd ſa hapnit throw curage ingliſmen doi v mekill deir ryſing worthy weir throw hurt vainis meniſching blude ȝit wyſe counſall gude februar wallace ſend apryll fra bownit wend bot gude ſeruice pleſance ſpace worthy auance ¶how wallace paſt watter irwyn tak fiſche cap vj sa ane tyme deſyrit play apryll thre twentie day irwyn watter fiſche tak went sic fantaſie fell intent leid net ane chyld yair ȝeid bot none ane felloun dreid ſword left ſa neuer agane gude ſuppois ſufferit pane laubour nocht ſle happy tuik fiſche aboundantlie day ten houri ouir couth pa rydand thair come neir quhair wallace lord peirſe capitane yan air fra turnit couth glaſgow fair part court wallace laubour ſene yair raid fyne cled garment grene sanct martynis fiſche ſaid scot wald haif wallace agane yame meikly anſwer gaif war reſſoun think ȝe ſuld haue part waith ſuld delt place fre hart bad chyld gif yame waithing sutheroun ſaid thy deilling nocht tak thow wald gif v ſmall lychtit doun fra chyld tuik wallace ſaid gentil men gif ȝe leif v ſum part pray cheritie ane agit knicht ſeruis lady day gude freind leif part tak nocht away thow ſall haue leif fiſche tak mair forſuith ſall flitting fair ſerue ane lord thir fiſche ſall gang wallace anſwerit ſaid thow art wrang quhom thowis yow ſcot faith yow ſeruis ane blaw ran ane ſword cā draw william wa na wappinis thair bot polt ſtaf quhilk hand bair wallace faſt cheik tuik ſa gude quhill feit ſchuik ſword flaw fra ane fuit braid ye land wallace glaid hynt ſone hand ye ſword ane akwart ſtraik gaif vnder heid craig ſunder draif laif lychtit wallace na help bot goddis grace ather ſyde full faſt thay dang greit perrell gif thay leſtit lang vpon heid greit ire ſtraik ane ſcheirand ſword glaid collair bane ane vther hit arme haiſtely quhill hand ſword baith ye land ly tother twa fled thair hors agane ſtikkit yat laſt plane thre ſlew thair twa fled yair micht efter thair lord bot ſicht takand mure thay culd twyn yai raid anone yai wald blyn cryit abyde ȝour men ar martyrit doun richt cruelly fals regioun fyue ȝour men heir watter baid fiſche ȝow bring thocht na proffeit maid ar eſchaipit bot feild ſtane ar thre lord ſpeirit mony micht thay ſaw bot ane he ouircūmin v leuch lord ſaid ſoull mot ȝow fall sen ane ȝow he put confuſioun quha menis maiſt ye deuill hell droun day faith beis nocht ſocht quhen wallace yus ye worthy work wrocht thair hors tuik geir yat left thair gaif ouir ye craft ȝeid fiſche na mair went eme • ald deid wo neir worthit weid ſaid ſone thir tythandis ſittis ſoir yai knawin yow may tak ſkaith yair foir vncle ſaid na langer byde thir sutheroun hors lat ſe gif ryde bot ane chyld ſeruice mak emis ſone wald nocht tak gude knicht ſaid deir couſing pray quhen thow wantis gude • ū feche auouch siluer gold gart ane geif wallace inc • ynit lawly tuik leif ☞ ✚ ☜ ¶the secund buik declairis wallace ſlew churll awin ſtaf air cap j ȝoung wallace yan fulfillit hie curage pryis armis deſyrous vaſſalage thy vaſſalage may neuer forlorne thy deid knawin yocht ye warld ſworne thy haill mynd laubour beſynes ſet weir verray richteouſnes felloun lois thy deir worthy kin rancour mair remanis thy mynd within lyfe maiſt part fude ſe yame ſched ye byrnand sutheroun blude ouchtirhous withouttin mair raid bot ſchort tyme peice yair abaid thair ane wallace yat welcūmit full weill thocht ingliſmen yairof lytill feill baith meit drink thair laglane wod quhen maid repair gentill man full oft refeit ſtuf hous full oft beit sa deſyrit toun air ſe chyld na tuik ay nixt wod▪ wallace gart leif hors syne ſuit ȝeid mercat cro peirſe caſtell air ingliſmen greit number repair toun reulling yair awin wyſe mony scot yai full greit ſuppryſe abaiſſing wallace amang thame ȝeid rage ȝouth maid haue na dreid ane churll thay yat felloun burdingis bair exceidingly wald lift mekill mair ony thre yat yai amang thame fand al ane ſport tuik hand bure ane ſting ane buſteous poill braid bak ony wald thoill bot ane groit al faſt micht draw quhen wallace hard ſpeik mery ſaw deſyrit mercat ane ſtraik bad groitis thre churll grantit proffer fane pay ſiluer wallace full bane wallace ſting tuik vp hand full ſturdely befoir couth ſtand wallace vpon bak gaif quhill rig bane ſunder draif carll deid ſpeik na mair ingliſmen aſſemblit wallace thair feill feild folkis fecht faſt vnabaiſit nocht greitly agaſt vpon heid ſting ane hit quhill bane brayne gart pecis fle ane vther ſtraik ane baſnet ſteill tre thair raif fruſchit euerilk deill ſting tynt ingliſman deid craig bane brokin ſteid drew ane ſword helpit neid throw thickeſt preis ȝeid hors full fane wald haue bene twa ſairit maiſt yat cruell kene wallace returnit man mekill mane ane ſtraik formeſt be ſlane ane felloun ſtraik ye tother gat tyde gude ſword gart thair abyde corſlait brymlie bair groundin ſword throw body ſchair fyue ſlew thair paſt fra toun gat hors laglane maid boun keipit chyld leit nocht abyde eſchaipit thus laglane ryde feill followit hors al fute tak wallace na bute treis thick keipit full weill bot thair byde yat couth nocht adeill gude ordinance yat effeirit ſtait cuſtume tyme baith air lait squyar wallace ouchterhous yat baith bed meit maid pa tyme remanit thair bot ſair langit ſe toun air thidder paſt vpon ane mercat day wald god biddin away emis ſeruand fiſche ſend schir rānald craufurd yt ſchiref yan kend ¶how wallace ſlew lord peirſeis stewart tane preſonit air cap ij qvhen tane ſic gude bocht peirſeis stewart richt ſadly ſocht ſaid thow scot quhome byis thow thing ye schiref ſaid heuinis king lord ſall haue ſyne ga feche mair wallace cace neir gangand thair ȝeid ſaid deir freind pray schireffis ſeruand yat yow wald lat ane lordly man stewart blude thocht wallace chargit termis rude ga hyne yow scot ye mekill deuill ſpeid thy schireffis vſe thow wenis v leid ane hunting ſtaf hand bair thair ſmoit william wallace thair bot tre full lytill ſonȝe maid faſt collair claucht withoutti • baid ane felloun knyif faſt hart ſtraik syne fra deid ſchot richt ſuddandlie catour ſen ſyne trow na mair ingliſmen aſſemblit wallace thair four ſcoir war ſet armour burneiſt boun mercat day scottis keip toun wallace baldly drew ane ſword weir birny formeſt couth beir throw body ſtikkit deid ſindrie paſt • ra ſteid ane vther akwart ane lang ſtraik tuik thair vpon kne ye bane ſunder ſchair thrid ſtruik ane peſane mailȝe craig twa na weidis micht auailȝe thus wallace fairi al wod ane lyoun ingliſmen war bargane boun thay keip gait ſpeiris rude lang dynt ſword na man micht gang wallace harneſt body weill thay ſocht ſchairp ſwordis ſteill fra ſtrenth inueronit throw preis ane ſyde brak vnto ane well ſtude ſey ſyde weill wo thair muſt neid abyde part yair ſpeiris pecis thair ſchair fra ye caſtell vther help come mair ouir dyke yai glaid ather ſyde brak doun wall na ſuccour tyde wallace wiſt na wane bot de wyn deid amang thame thus ȝeid he▪ vther part greit ire heuand faſt byrneiſt brand bryſtit laſt brak hyltis away blaid flew wiſt na wane bot furth knyif drew firſt ſlew quhilk hand he hynt vther twa ſtikkit dynt remanent ſpeiris he ſocht bure ground farther micht nocht lordis bad yai ſuld nocht ſla pyne mair thay chargit ta thair innis ſuppois yat ſworne gait force thay haue borne thus gude wallace ingliſmen tane falt help allane culd nocht ceis curage ſa bair freuoll fortoun he brocht ſnair thir fals goddes full vnrichteouſnes fals iuno full dowbilnes thay fenȝeit goddes ȝit wallace neuer knew greit rychteouſnes ay mercy drew kyn micht nocht get na kin thing micht thay haue payit • ra • ſoun ane king mair thay bad mair vane yair beſt men yat day ſeuin he ſlane thay gart ſet intill ane preſoun fell torment greit pietie tell euill meit drink yai gart vnto geif greit meruell gif micht lang thair leif eik thairto preſoun law quhill yai thocht tyme hald law leif thus panefull ſteid quhill god abuif ſend ſum remeid plane complaint pieteous womenting wofull weiping yat taking tormenting euerie creature allace thay ſaid ſall lyfe indure flour ȝouth tender age fortoun armis he left thirlage leuand day ane chiftane haue nane durſt tak hand bot ȝoung wallace allane land loiſt claucht ſnair apercy scotland greit cair ¶how wallace preſonit air eſchaipit cap iij barrellit hering watter yai gaif quhair ſet vgly caif sic fude febill commend ſaid thus gif god wald reſſaif pieteous spreit ſaull ouir laif cairfull lyfe may nocht defend ouir sutheroun vnto de • th drew rew deid verray trew ſone warld wend gif ſuld preſoun mak ane end ¶eternall god quhy ſuld yus wyis die sen beleif haill remanis thy archearis hardy war wicht amang scottis bikkerit thair micht thair awfull ſchot felloun byde wallace men thay woundit feill tyde thame ſicker archery better thay war thay gat euin party feild byde outher ſword ſpeir wallace perſauir men tuik mekill deir gart thame change ſtand yat ſteid keſt alwayis ſaif thame fra deid full greit trauell vpon ſelf tuik sutheroun archearis feill men gart de longcaſtell schyre bowmē war yat place ane fair archear ay waittit wallace ane oppin quhair vſit repair drew ane ſicker ſchot ſair vnder chyn throw ane collar ſteill left ſyde hurt hals ſum deill aſtoneiſt bot nocht greitly agaſt fra men followit faſt turning gude he tane vpon craig ſunder ſtraik bane feill thame na freindſchip fand fyftene day ſchot deit hand arrowis waiſtit war gane inglis ordinance heir nane chois bot outher de haue richt happyer may ſall chaip grace land lorane reddy hand efter none day feill men wit counſall ſone ȝeid thay sutheroun keſt ſchairply euerilk ſyde ſaw ye micht ingliſmen yat worthy war wicht schir iohne buttellar releuit agane synderit ye scottis yame mekill pane lorane al cruell kene ane ſair aſſay forſuith yair micht ſene ye ſtrenth yai micht na langer byde raynge ſa ſtrang come vpon ather ſyde ye thickeſt wod yai maid thair fell defence aganis thair fais ſa full violence richt feill sutheroun leuit thair lyfe wed ane new ſtrenth wallace men fled thair aduerſaris thay maid full feill debait bot help yame ſelf nane vther ſuccour yai wait sutheroun al war ſynderit twyn bot thay agane togidder ſone wyn full ſubtelly thair ordinance thay maid mē deid thay knew wallace ſtrenth par • thay ſet breid lenth ſex hundreth weill graithit thair armis likly men wreik thame thair harmis ane hundreth men chargit armis ſtrang keip ane hound thay thame hundreth mē wallace ſa weill vpon tuik tyde throw greit preis maid ane way ful wyde helpand scottis deir worthy hand fell famen left fey vpon land ȝit wallace loiſt fyftene ſteid fourtie men sutheroun thair war deid butellaris folk ſa fruſchit war deid hardy ſcottis ſtrenthis throw yai ȝeid vpon tay ſyde thay haiſtit thame full faſt thay war watter haue paſt better thocht perrell vpon land wilfully ſe men drowne quhair reſkew mycht nane agane ire feild ar thay gane butellar put men array thame ſet awfull hardy aſſay ather ſyde wappnis ſtif ſteill wallace agane na freindſchip leit thame feill bot de thay wiſt na mair ſuccour thus fend thay lang ſtalwart ſtour scottis chiftane ȝoung ane rage vſit weir fechtis curage▪ ſaw men sutheroun tak ſic wrang thame reuenge dreidles gang maid faudoun left beſyde thame land power come ſuddanly fand thair ſluith hound graith way ȝeid vther tred ſcho tuik na heid ſluith ſtoppit faudoun ſtill ſcho ſtude na forther wald fra tyme ſcho fand blude ingliſmen demit vther yai couth tell bot yat ye scottis fochtin amang yame ſell richt wa thay war loiſſit thair ſent wallace twa men amang oiſt went diſſimulit weill na man ſuld thame ken richt tuke tyme remufe ¶how wallace paſt lochmabane thay cuttit hors taillis ſchaif blude latter ca ij syne gilbank paſt nicht vpon ye morne four mē dicht corheid without reſting raid quhair neuoy thom haliday abaid edward lytill al cou • ing deir quhilk • blyith quhen wiſt ſa neir thankand greit god ſend thame ſaif agane mony demit stratherne ſlane gude cheir thay maid thay dayis thre wallace ſaid deſyrit ſe lochmabane toun ingliſmen yat yair feird day thay bownit thame fair sextene gudly cheualry knok wod leifit bot thre thomas haliday went town edward lytill keirly maid thame bown ane oiſtler thomas haliday led yame richt gaif command yair denner ſuld dicht heir ane me gude intent thay ȝeid ingliſmen thay trowit thair na dreid ane cliffurd come emis sone lord thre treuth record thair innis ſone efter wallace paſt quha aucht thay hors greit hething aſt· gude wyfe ſaid haue pleiſt beſt thre gentill men ar cūmin weſt quha deuill thame maid ſa gaylie ryde faith ane wed thair mon abyde thir lewit scottis he leirit lytill gude lo thair hors ar ſchent fault blude greit ſcorne outtin wordis mair taillis thay thre hors thay ſchair gude wyfe cryit pieteouſly couth greit sa wallace come couth capitane meit ane woman tauld thay hors ſchent proper ire grew matalent followit faſt ſaid gude freindis abyde seruice tak thy craft tyde marchell thow art without command reward agane think ſuld pay sen lait new come weſt countrie ane barbour beſt cut ſchaif ane wounder gude thow ſall feill vſe lat blude gude ſword capitane he tane quhill hors agane merchellit neuer nane ane vther ſone vpon heid freſche hors rydand full haiſtely seuin ſcoir cumpany scottis lap quhen thay power ſaw frawart ſouth thame thocht beſt draw wallace ſaid na wit weir power byde thame bargane heir ȝ • ne ar gude men thre ſlew thair ſpeir gane thus gude ſword hand he tane dang derf • ſtraikis ſad ſair quhome hit greuit scottis na mair fra sutheroun men naturall reſſoun knew ane ſtraik ay ane man ſlew meruellit thay ſa mekill mane thair beſt man kynd ſlane greit ſtrenth agane helpit nocht nane vther incontrair wallace ſocht ſaid thay leif ſtrenth vntane haill kinrik wyn allane thay left feild thair power twentie war tynt morland al thairfoir wald nocht ſtynt bot followit faſt thre hundreth dreid ſwore ſuld vengit deid scottis wan hors becauſe yair awin couth faill fleing ſyne cheiſit maiſt auaill feild thus wicht wallace gane gude men loiſſit ane fyue woundit war lichtly furth thay raid wallace ane ſpace behind yame ay abaid halyday preuit weill mony place siſter sone gude wallace warly thay raid held thair hors aynd thay trowit weill sutheroun wald affaynd haill power atanis thame ſet bot wallace keſt thair purpois let brek thair ray veſyit full faſt ingliſmen ſa greitly agaſt nane thame durſt ruſche ſtaill array togidder held thame haill sutheroun ſaw abandounly wallace abaid neir hand thair cheualry morlandis hors yai knew woūder weill paſt thair lord tauld euer ilk deill lo schir thay ſaid forſuith ȝone ſame handis garris ſa mony de haue hors grace vpon feit byde doutis nocht throw fyue thouſand ryde reid ȝe ceis follow na mair dreid repent ſyne full ſair blamit thame ſaid men may weill ſe cowartis ȝe ar ſa wald fle thair counſall ȝit leif wald thame nocht greit ire thame ſadly ſocht waillād ane place quhair yai micht bargane mak wallace wa vpon tak ſa byde thame ane plane wallace schir iohne ye grahame met richt gudly hūbilnes gret perdoun aſkit reprufe • oir chace ſaid ſuld moir informatioun mak ſa gude quhen schir iohne wallace weill vnderſtude way ſaid yairof na day done approchand nicht wallace thay aſkit counſall richt anſwerit thus ſpeik bot ȝour leif richt laith war ony gude man greif bot thus ſay termis ſchort wald aſſaill gif ȝe think may lochmabane hous quhilk left allane weill wait power nane carlauerok al ȝit maxwell he hand thay micht baith ane wand aganis sutheroun he countrie say quhat ȝe beſt think schir iohne grahame gaif firſt gude cō ſent syne ye laif richt ane hail intent lochmabane richt haiſtely thay ryde quhen yai come yair nocht half ane myle beſyde nicht mirk counſall ar thay gane mone sterne apperance yair nane wallace ſaid think land reſt thom haliday thow knawis countrie beſt heir na noyis feill folk heir thairfoir trow ar le dout haliday ſaid tak ane ryde befoir maner ſe watſone callit thow mak bown yame thow ay nichtbour yi town grant thame aganis myne intent euer thame ill vnto ȝet thay twa peirtly furth raid portar come without langer abaid iohne watſone tythingis culd ſpeir oppin bad capitane cūmis neir ȝe • mair vnwyſely vp drew thom haliday ſone craig threw ane knyfe ſtikkit deid ane dark hoill doun dreidles keſt deid iohne watſone he hynt keyis hand portar yā wicht wallace cūmand thay enterit befoir thame fand na except wemen ſimpill ſeruandis twa kiching lang ſcudlaris thay bene sone thay war ſlane quhen lady ſene scho cryit grace deit tre wallace ſaid madame ȝour noyis lat wemen ȝit bot lytill euill ȝoung childer lyke nocht ſpill wald haue meit haliday quhat ſayis thow faſtand folk dyne gude tyme war greit pur • iance ordanit thame befoir baith breid aill gude wyne vther ſtoir meit thay bownit thay faſtit lang gude men armis vnto clois gart gang part fleand folk fute thay fra thame glaid knok heid quhair greit melle maid ay thay come iohne watſone leit thame done deith without noyis din na man left thair ingland borne caſtell weill thay veſyit morne iohnſtoun ſend ane man gude degre secund dochter forſuith weddit halidayis deir neuoy wallace greit capitane thay maid place thay left thair ane gude array syne iſchit furth vpon ſecund day wemen leif ingland fair schir iohne ye grahame gude wallace culd cair corheid ludgit yame yat nicht vpon morne sone hicht efter denner thair armour cleir ganeſt way thame approchit neir wallace ſaid ſone thay na ingliſmen oiſt gaitis weill thay ken thom halyday thay men gydit richt annandaill led thame nicht twa gude sonnis iohnſtoun man cokburnis peth gaddering maid dunbar wald cum withouttin baid lawder ſaid war beſt think fa •• er pa dunbar wallace anſwerit may laiſer ryde ȝone power thinkis bargane byde ane thing ȝe ſall weill vnderſtand ane hardyer lord nocht land micht maid trew ſteidfaſt ane king wit force mekill thing bot wilfully lykis tyne ſell thus raid thay furth wald na langer dwell eiſt dunbar quhair men thame tald cace erll patrik warnit wallace neir innerwik cheiſit ane feild waill nyne hundreth lyklie men waill four hundreth wallace richt thay anone approchit thair ſicht greit falt thair gude tretie betuene mak concord full ſone ſene without reheirs actioun tyde ather part togidder faſt thay ryde ſtour ſtrang wounder perrillous contenit lang deidis cheualrous mony thair deit cruell scottis blude tretie mater nocht gude thairfoir ceis tell diſtructioun pietie ane natioun bot erll patrik feild left laſt richt cokburnis peth yair paſt aggreuit ſair men thus tynt wallace returnit wald na langer ſtynt towart dunbar quhair ſuithfaſt men tald na purueyance left hald man fence bene thair lord quhen wallace hard ſicker trew record dunbar tuik haill bandoun gaif keip criſtall setoun quhilk ſtuffit weill men gude vittaill vpon morne wallace wald nocht faill thre hundreth cokburnis peth ſocht erll patrik iſchit byde wald nocht sone park wallace ane range he ſet bonkill wod corſpatrik fled let norhame paſſit quhen wallace ſaw micht na better caldſtreme raid ludgeit tweid erll patrik haiſt ſpeid paſſit wallace power rais without reſting ettrik foreſt gais wallace followit bot wald nocht aſſaill ane range mak micht nocht vaill quir ſtrenth thick ſtrang twelf myle breid thairto twyis al lang cokholme erll patrik baid reſt mair power wallace paſt weſt erll patrik graithit haiſtelie ingland paſt get thair ſupple throw land richt eirniſtly cout pa anthonie beik lord durame wallace put glaſgow befoir ſlew perſe thair malice moir biſchop beik gart ſone greit power ryſe northumbirland vpon ane awfull wyſe thay ordanit bruce scotland pa wyn awin bot euill diſſauit thay gart trow wallace rebell thocht tak kinrik ſell fals thay war euer ȝit he bene lawtie treuth euer wallace ſene fend ye richt tuik hand thocht bring bruce fre land mater tary nocht ſtrang power sutheroun togidder ſocht fra oyis watter aſſemblit haill tweid land oiſt threttie thouſand deid themis mouth ſend schippis ſee keip dunbar nane ſuld thame ſupple erll patrik paſt twentie thouſand let befoir dunbar ane ſtalwart seige ſet biſhop beik robert bruce baid ſtill ten thouſand norame thair wallace faſt lauborand louthiane come gude meu fyue thouſād richt weill beſene thair armour bricht thocht reſkew setoun bald wicht vnder ȝeſter firſt nicht ludgeit hay come ane gude cheualrie doun foreſt tyme bene cūming sutheroun ſene fyftie wiſe men weir thay tald wallace patrikis greit affeir hay ſaid forſuith ȝe micht ouirſet power agane richt ſone may nocht get counſall gif battall thankit comfort counſall ſaid freind hay caus wend sa wyn rek nocht end richt ſuith ani mon de richt quha ſuld terrour erll patrik thair ane meſſinger gart pa tald anthonie beik wallace cūmand tythingis biſchop full glaid ane mendis full fane wald haue mair prolong throw laumyr mure yai raid neir spot mure buſchment ſtill baid quhair erll patrik ordanit wallace beik vnwarnit ȝit befoir nocht haiſtie deid bot put baith dreid vpon ſwyft hors ſcurriouris raid betuene cūming erll patrik he ſene hous left mure gane ane plane feild thair oiſt he tane gude setoun ſyne iſchit menȝe part men dunbar left wallace raid richteous ſyde gude array spot mure thay ryde sum scottis dred erll ſa mony twentie thouſand agane ſa pa bot iop perſauit bad wallace ſuld byde tyne nocht ȝour men bot ſum ſtrenth ȝe ryde ſall pa get ȝow power mair thir ar ouir gude thus lichtly wair wallace ſaid treuth nocht fle four ay ane quhill may ar ouir neir ſic purpois tak ane dangerous chace thay micht vpon v mak heir twentie power day wald aſſay ſuppois war away mony thay ar goddis ſaik ſtrang ȝone sutheroun folk ſtour wil byde lāg ☞ ✚ ☜ ¶how corſpatrik brocht scotland biſchop beik robert bruce wallace gaif thame battell put thame scotland ca ij bryme battell braithly ather ſyde greit reird yair rais ouir quhair yat yai ryde ſair ſēblie quhē yai togidder met feill ſtraikis thair thay ſadly vther ſet prunȝeand ſpeiris throw plaitis peirſit faſt mony hors doun ground thay caſt sadillis thay teym hors maiſteris thair ſouth ſyde fyue thouſand doun thay bair gude wallace oiſt formeſt cūmerit ſa quhill yat laif away ga erll patrik baid ſa cruell intent haill oiſt tuik hardiment aganis wallace mony ſtour wallace knew weill men wald nocht fle na power leuand lyfe quhill thay heill micht ay ane fyfe greit ſtryfe mony handillit hair feill dyntis cruell hard debait feirs ſtryking maid mony ane greuous woūd vpon eird blude maid abound wallace oiſt ane compas baid quhair ſa thay turnit full greit ſlauchter yai maid wallace grahame ramſay full worthy bald setoun richard lundy adam wallace al ricardtoun baith hay lyle gude men renoun boyd barklay baird lawder yat wicht feill ingliſmen derſly deith thay dicht bot erll patrik full feirſly faucht agane throw awin hand mony put pane men thrang ford wart thra maid throw oiſt feill ſloppis fra ingliſmen began planely fle biſchop beik full ſuddandly thay ſe robert bruce contrair natiue men wallace wa fra tyme couth ken brucis deidis aggreuit mair laif day ſemblit thair greit buſchment atanis brak breid ten thouſand haill douchtie war deid flearis erll patrik releuit thay faucht agane quhair mony war miſcheuit quhen wallace ſaw buſchment brokin feild hors thay thocht pa bot ſaw weill oiſt ſound thair weid thocht fray formeſt ȝeid new cūmin oiſt thame ſemblit yair ather ſyde ſtraikis ſad ſair worthy scottis ſa feirſly faucht agane anthonis men mony haue thay ſlane bot tyran ſa vſit weir wallace oiſt thay full mekill deir bald bruce ſa cruelly wrocht throw ſtrenth hand feill scottis gart de reſiſt bruce wallace preiſſit faſt bot ingliſmen ſa thick betuix thame paſt erll patrik haiſt mocht throw ſtour wallace ſone ſocht peſane ane felloun ſtraik gaif keruit plait ſcharp groundit glaif throw ſtuf woundit ſum deill bot wallace thocht ſuld vengit weill followit ane ſtraik ettillit faſt bot ane maitland rekleſly betuix thame past vpon ye heid gude wallace he tane throw heid braune ſunder ſtraik bane deid ground ſtraik draif thus wallace diſſeuerit fra laif gude men amang thame allane ſocht feill enemeis mony ane stikkit hors ground behuiſit licht fend himſelf al wyſelie micht worthy scottis micht na langer byde ſair hartis feild thay ryde thame feir thay weind wallace bene fuit amang enemeis kene gude roume maid breid gude ſword helpit neid nane ſa ſtrang gat ane ſtraik efter agane maid neuer ane scot wraik erll patrik greit craft weir ſpeiris ordanit gude wallace doun beir anew thay tuik haill feild thay ȝeid thocht ſuld haue na beild ather ſyde faſt prunȝeand geir hewit heidis wyſelie couth weir worthy scottis full lytill wiſt socht gude grahame quhē yai yair chiftane miſt lawder lyle hay yat ful wicht bald ramſay quhilk ane worthy knicht lundy boyd criſtall setoun fyue hundreth war bargane boun reſkew full ruidly thay raid wallace ane large roume thay maid biſchop beik braithly borne eird reſkew thair ane felloun reird gat vp feill sutheroun thay ſlew preis wallace thay reſkew sone horſit vpon ane cuirſer wicht towart ane ſtrenth rydis thair micht richt wyſelie fled reſkewand mony man erll patrik ſtuf chace began ſlearis thair lytill harme thay wrocht gude wallace folk away togidder ſocht thir fyue hundreth ye quhilk ſpak air sa awfully abandounit thame ſair na followar durſt fra fellow ga gude flearis ſic turning thay four thouſand haill tane ſtrenth befoir wallace oiſt comfort moir glaſtaden foreſt thocht hald erll patrik turnit thocht neuer ſa bald agane beik quhen chaipit wallace curſſand fortoun miſchancefull cace feild wan ſeuin thouſand loiſt deid day biſchoppis boiſt wallace men fyue hundreth ſlane ge bot na chiftane murning le neir euin bot beik wald nocht abyde laumyr mute thay turnit tyde thair ludgeingtuik quhair thocht maiſt auaill weill trowit scottis wald aſſaill vpon feild quhair thay gaif battell laſt cuntrie men wallace gadderit faſt edinburgh craufurd wicht four hundreth come thair armour bricht wallace raid ludgeing tane teuidaill come gude men mony ane iedburgh rothuen tyde togidder ſocht fra mony diuers ſyde schir williame yan yat lord dowglas four ſcoir nicht come wallace twentie hundreth new men met nicht vpon yair fais venge thame thair micht firſt feild thir gude men nocht bene wallace wachis thair aduerſaris he ſene quhat wyſe thay thair ludgeing maid wallace bownit efter supper baid laumyr mute thay paſſit haiſtely sone array ȝeid gude cheualry wallace thame maid twa partis schir iohne ye grahame setoun ordanit lawder hay thre thouſand ryde ſelf laif tuik wyſelie gyde lundy baith ramſay dowglace barklay boyd gude adam wallace day approchit wounder neir bricht titan preſence appeir scottis oiſt ſone ſemblit ſicht thair enemeis thay war nocht reddy dicht array feill sutheroun richt awfully wallace thame pa entre scottis ſa weill thame bair feill thair fais deith brytinuit thair redles thay rais mony fled away sum ground ſmoirit quhair yai lay greit noyis cry raiſit thame amang gude grahame come yat ſtalwart ſtrāg fra wallace men war weill togidder met south part ſa awfully thay ſet incontrair thame thay frayit folk micht ſtād atanis thair fled sutheroun ten thouſand worthy scottis wrocht vpon ſic ane wyſe iop ſaid ſelf yat yai war mekill pryſe ȝit biſchop beik felloun tyran ſtrang baid ſtour richt awfully lang ane knicht skeltoun cruell kene befoir ſtuid armour ſchene fend lord full worthely wrocht lundy ſaw ſadly ſocht gude ſword ane akwart ſtraik gaif throw peſane ſtuf craig ſunder draif quhair laif war ſtoneiſt ſteid bald skeltoun lundyis hand deid fled thay micht na langer byde patrik beik away bruce ryde fyue thouſand held ane ſlop away norhame hous haiſt thay may men followit worthy war wicht mony flear derfly deith thay dicht thir thre lordis caſtell thay ſocht full feill thay loiſſit ingland brocht iourney twentie thouſand thay tynt drownit ſlane ſpeir ſwordis dynt scottis tweid haiſtit thame ſa faſt feill sutheroun men wrang fuirdis thay paſt wallace returnit norhame quhen yai wair worthy bruce hart wounder ſair leuer haue large fre till crown fyne gold charge mair yan troy quhen ye greikis wan wallace paſſit mony awfull man ouir patrikis land waiſtit wounder faſt tuik greit gudis placis doun caſt ſteidis twelf met hamys cald wallace gart brek thay buirly biggingis balo baith mers al louthiane except dunbar ſtandand leuit nane edinburgh vpon aucht day vpon morne wallace without delay perth paſt quhair ane counſall ſet barrounis ſchewit withouttin let greit vow richt weil eſchewit ane maiſter gart erll patrik pa becaus ſaid scotland held nocht king edward get ſupple ſocht lord blyith welcūmit weill wallace thankand greit god fair happy cace wallace tuik ſtait gouerne scotland barnage haill maid ane oppin band delt land gude men scotlandis richt ſet yair lyfis dout stanetoun gaif lawder wage knicht wallange aucht heritage birgem cruik gaif lyle yat wicht skrymgeour al full gude rewaird dicht syne wallace toun vther landis yair till worthy men delt nobill awin kyn heritage nane gaif bot office haill euerilk man micht ſe couetiſe thair couth na man blame baid rewaird quhill king ſuld cum hame thocht byde law befoir king maiſter quhen ſaw scotland blyith dolour bene lang ilk ane part gude laubour thay gang ¶how wallace paſt ingland remanit yair thre quarteris ane ȝeir come hame agane battell ca iij tyme october paſt nouember neir approchit wounder faſt tythingis thair come king edward greuit power scotlād thocht pa erll patrik geuin ſic counſall wallace gat wit ſemblit power haill fourtie thouſand roſlyng mure thair met lordis ſaid king edwardis ſet contrair richt ſeik v land hecht god ȝow hand ſall meit greit barnage within ingland fend heritage fals deſyre ſall ſelf ſene ſall v find incontrair ene sen wrang he riddin regioun ſall pa incontrair crown nocht bid greit lordis v fair myne intent planely declair purpois outher wyn de quha ȝeildis ſall neuer ranſonit barrounis anſwerit worthely ſaid thay wald pa thair cheualry ſelf iop prouydit menȝe twentie thouſand waillit men tuik harnes hors gart amang thame waill wappinnis anew micht thame awaill graithit thir men cruell war kene better weir warld couth nocht ſene bad laif laubour byde gude array fra roſſing mure thay ryde yair muſter gude wallace couth thame quhat myſteris ane power pa ane trow ſet ar plane battell nocht diſcomfeiſt realme pure waiſtit sutheroun blude go wyn yame gold vther gude oiſt inclynit humbill ſaid thay ſuld bidding fulfill erll malcolme ireland men gane bot name reull wald tak nane wallace knew ane lord yat worthy counſall wrocht full ſteidfaſtly starker gif thay battell ſene befoir gude iournayis bene ane man ſtrenth he gude wit ane haill regioun may comfort call manly hector wrocht weir aganis ane hundreth comptit ſpeir bot nocht throw ſtrenth anerly sic reull led nobill cheualry thir exemplis war worthy ken hector leif ſpeik furth men knicht campbell maid veyage lochow cheif heritage gude ramſay furth iourney went schir iohne grahame fordwart intent wallace couſing adam full worthy robert boyd furth blyithly yai pa baith auchinlek richard lundy lawder hay setoun full worthy royall oiſt reſting furth thay raid brokis feild yair ane quhyle yai baid thā wallace tuik fourty lei roxburgh ȝet raid ſone wald ceis sutheroun meruellit gif ſuld wallace without aſſouerance come perſew place schir rauf gray ſone preſence couth warnit thus farther wald pa purpois ingland ryde na tyme haif seiſſing byde tak tent heir cūming agane gif ouir hous ſend keyis plane thus command befoir thir witnes large gif thow nocht remane charge bot done throw force tak ouir wall thow ſall hangit hie turnit oiſt wend ilk command berwik ſone ſend gude ramſay yat ane worthy knicht oiſt mair full awfully dicht began tweid ſpairit nocht thay fand bot brynt force haill northumberland durame toun thay brynt vp ane gleid abbayis thay ſpairit kirkis quhair yat yai ȝeid ȝork thay raid baid thay wald blyn byrne ſlay thame thocht na ſyn na ſin thay thocht ſamin lat v feill bot williame wallace quit querrell weill forthis thay wan ſmall caſtellis keſt doun aſper wappinnis payit thair ranſoun preſoneris thay lykit nocht keip quhome yai ouir tuik thay maid thair freindis weip na ſutheroūſauit yair greit rich ſic truſtrie callit bot wretchitnes vnto ȝettis subuerbis toun braithly yai brynt brak yair biggingis doun wallis aſſailȝeit fyftene dayis quhil king edward ſcud yame wayis ane knicht ane clerk ane squyar pei prayit fair byrning ceis hecht battell fyftene dayis war paſt souerance ſa lang gif lykit aſt al ſpeirit quhy wallace tuik hand felloun ſtryfe defence scotland ſaid meruellit wit thy aganis ingland ſa greit party sen ȝe haue maid mekill scotland fre war gude tyme lat malice wallace he hard meſſage ſay thair manly voce richt thus ſaid thame • il ȝe may knaw weill richt aneuch haif souerance keip nocht craif becaus ane natiue scottis man det fend kingrik dangering deſyre grant ſum thing oiſt ſall ceis chance may betyde thir fyftene dayis bargane abyde ſall nocht le mufe ȝow reſpite ſelf couth neuer trow king edwardis writ vnder seill yai gaif fourtie dayis thay ſuld battelll hait wallace gaif credence thair king thair leif thay tuik ſyne paſſit reſting tald haill wallace leit thame feill yair souerance keipit nocht adeill sic reullit men ſa awfull effeir ar nocht criſtinit leidis weir king anſwerit ſaid ſuld kend cūmis wit enemeis commend thay ar dreid richt greitly certane sadly thay think harmis thay haue tane leif thame thus counſall thair king scottis agane ſpeik ſum thing vallace tranoyntit vpon ſecund day fra ȝork yai paſt richt ane gude array north weſt yai went battell buſkit boun thair ludgeing tuik beſyde northallartoun cryit peax thair mercatis ſtand thay fourtie dayis pepill ingland quha lykit ony vittall ſell thair ſchoir war mekill tell schir rauf rymont capitane miltoun greit power nicht ordanit pa wallace oiſt mak ſum ieopardie feill scottis men dwelt countrie wiſt thing gadderit wallace thay maid wyſe felloun cace gude lundy callit thair hew ye hay lochorquhart air thre thouſand yat worthely wrocht syne priuatly fra oiſt thay ſocht men tuik come new gydis thay cuntrie knew oiſt maid gude quyet ane ſpace fra thame buſkit priuatlie schir rauf rymōt ſeuin thouſand come wallace oiſt ane ieopardie begin buſchment brak thay oiſt come neir sutheroun men ye worthy scottis cā ſ • eir thre thouſand hail war braithly brocht groūd iourney thay ſocht ſickerly he found schir rauf rymont ſtikkit ane ſpeir thre thouſand ſlane worthy war weir sutheroun wiſt quhen thair chiftane ſlane miltoun faſt yai fled thair mane wallace followit gude cheualry amang sutheroun thay enterit ſuddanly scottis inglis toun atanis sutheroun men ſchot braithly keſt doun ſtanis thair awin men richt feill thair haue yai ſlane scottis war mekill mane vp greiſſis ran ſeiſit toun derfly deith sutheroun dang thay doun wallace thair he fundin full greit rich iowellis gold wappinnis harnes spulȝeit toun wyne vittaill oiſt ſend cariage greit waill thre dayis ſtill within toun baid syne brak doun werk worthely maid wyfis barnis thay put toun na man ſauit natioun quhen scottis tane turſit thair deſyre wallis thay brak ſet laif fyre tymmer werk thay brynt vp plane feird day oiſt raid agane gart caſt ane dyke micht ſum ſtrenthing keip oiſt fra ſuddand ieopardie ingliſmen richt greitly agaſt fra north south vnto thair king yai paſt punfrayt lay held ane parliament gif battell lordis couth nocht conſent bot wallace war scotland crownit king thair counſall fand ane perrillous thing thocht thay wan thay wan bot thay wair gif thay tynt loiſt ingland euer mair cace war put scottis hand decreit thair wit amang thame fand gif wallace wald vpon tak crown gif battaill thay ſuld reddy boun ſamin meſſage thay ſend agane thair intent thay tald plane wallace thame chargit fra preſence abſent counſall callit ſchew thame intent men deſyrit battell haif ony wyſe ingland ouir laif ſelf ſaid firſt war ane ouir hie thing aganis faith reif richteous king man borne natiue scotland weir crown nocht tak hand ſend realme det ſkill lat god abone reward sum bad wallace vpon tak crown wyſe men ſaid nay war deriſicun crown king voce parliament thay wiſt nocht gif scotland wald conſent vther ſone ſaid wrangous place thus demit thay mony diuers cace knicht campbell wit ane worthy man ſaid air thame preſent hard anſwerit quhen mony ſaid thair war beſt wald wallace grant thair till crown king solempnitly ane day get ane end lang delay gude erll malcolme ſaid yat wallace micht ane day fence scotlandis richt thocht refuiſſit leſtandly beir reſſaue crown feir weir pepill gaif thair conſent malcolme ald lord parliament ȝit wallace thoillit leit thame ſay yair quhen thay demit mony diuers ſkill awin mynd abhorrit thing cōmounis cryit mak wallace crownit king ſemblit ſaid ſuld nocht termis ſchort ȝe get na mair vnder cullour anſwer man mak bot ſic ane thing nocht tak ȝow ſuffer ſay ſwa war ane ſcorne crown ta thay wald nocht lat meſſage ingland cum thame amang thay ſuld vnderſtand twa knichtis paſt meſſage agane maid yame trow wallace crownt plane gart yame traiſt weil yat yi ſuithfaſt thing deliuerit thus thay paſſit king punfret went tald thay ſene wallace crownit quhairof yai lordis war tene barrat wox parliament quhair thay ſtude ſaid thay thir tythingis ar nocht gude ſa weill thir tymes befoir thair king mekill moir ane fortunate man na thing gais agane gif battell ſall repent pane ane vther ſaid battell haue ſtroy land na treſour may v ſaue conqueſt ſen firſt couth begyn ſellis nocht bot takis may wyn ingliſmen ſettis na dome bot deid price pennyis may mak v na remeid ane wodſtok ſayis ȝe wirk nocht wyſe gif ȝe tak anter ſuppryſe thocht wyn ar ingland laif ar ſtark aganis v ſtand wallace ſaif vther thay compt bot ſmall thy think war beſt keip ſtrenthis caſtellis wallit toun sa ſall fend folk regioun thocht north brynt better ſouerance ſet ingland ane ieopardie thay grantit wodſtok thame ſay thus thay put battell delay keſt thame haill vther gouernance aganis wallace wirk ſum ordinance thus wallace he plane diſcomfeiſt haill aganis king edward haill battall throw falſet ſubtilitie thay thocht ſuld greit neceſſitie falt fude ſteill land decreit thair wit amang thame fand thay gart king cry thair mercat doun fra trent tweid throuchfair fre toun thay boundis na man ſuld vittall leid sic ſtuf wyne vnder pane deid ſame decreit thay gaif parliament scottis furth ſpeik myne intent wallace lay ſtill quhill fourtie dayis war gane abydand thame bot apperance ſaw nane battell haue thair promeis doun thus ſailȝeit thay ilk ſyde greit micht day gane cūmin nicht wery oiſt drew thame fra toun set wachis reſting maid thame boun wiſch woundis wyne yame yat vnſoūd nane deid greit mirth yai aboūd suther • un micht mak arrayit agane thay began befoir toun thay ſailȝe wounder ſoir felloun ſchot ouir wallis full ſchene feill ingliſmen cruell war kene ſchot war ſlane thair targis ſtrang briſtit helmys mony ground thay dang brym byrnand fyre thay keſt euerie ȝet entres thus perrell oft thay ſet defendaris war full greit defence keipit thair toun throw ſtrenth violence thus day thay draif vnto nicht pauillounis bownit mony wery wicht irk weir toun ſtrang win artailȝe nobill men within quhen yai trowit ye scottis war reſt ieopardy ingliſmen thame keſt schir iohne mortoun knawin worthy wicht schir william lei graithit yame ye nicht fyue thouſand weill garniſt ſauage vpon scottis thay thocht mak ſkirmage ȝet iſchit haiſtely erll malcolme gude cheualry chak wache wallace ten he bene rydand he thair cūming ſene gart ane blaw cumpany reddy men arrayit thame haiſtely feill scottis ilk nicht harnes baid ordinance thay ſic reull maid ſchort auyſe togidder ar thay went vpon yair fais quhair feil sutheroū war ſchent wallace knew weill erll haiſtie thy ſped preis pa ane ſword weir hand bair firſt hit craig ſunder ſchair ane vther akwart face tuik baith neis front feild gart fle hardy erll befoir men paſt preis quhair feill war fechtand faſt ane ſcheirand ſword bair drawin hand firſt tey befoir fand quhen wallace togidder ſet thair leſt nane agane thame thay met bot outher deid elli ſtraikꝭ yat micht ye sutheroū 〈◊〉 ingliſmen fled▪ leit feild p • anely▪ worthy scottis wrocht thair ſa hardely schir iohne mortoun yat place deed▪ twelf hundreth ony mair remeid thir mony left feild ſlane laif returnit toun agan • rewit full ſair euer yai furth couth foūd amang yame full mony ane werkād wound oiſt agane ilk ane thair waird raid commandit wache na mair noyis maid bot reſtit ſtill quhill bricht day dew agane began toun ſailȝe new thus thay wrocht full greit worthynes aſſailȝeit ſair wit hardynes oiſtis vittall worth ſkant failȝeit faſt thus lay thay thair quhil diuers dayis war paſt land waiſtit meit nane win bot wiſt nocht folk within thay dred full ſair thair awin vernyſoun souerance prayit power toun ſpeik wallace thay deſyrit faſt appeirit ſpeirit quhat thay aſt mair anſwerit ſaid wald pay ranſoun pa ȝour way deir na mair toun greit ſchame war ſuld ȝoldin tounis haldin le power ȝe may nocht wyn v lang thocht yat ȝe byde ſall gif gold ȝe fra v ryde may gif battell durſt king sen he left war ouir hie ane thing v without ordinance toun hald gouernance wallace anſwerit ȝour gold rek nocht battell hidder ſocht leuer haue battell ingland gold gude king arthur fand mont michell quhen giant ſlew gold may gane bot worſchip ay new king promeiſt ſuld battell haif writ thairto vnder seill thay gaif letter band ȝe ſe may nocht auaill v tyme thocht gif battall think ſuld men wrokin vpon kyn mony greit wrang wrocht deuill lyke deid wrocht scotland maif ſaid schir richt thus vnderſtand haue na charge quhat king garris v bot kynd ſall bound ȝow sum part gold gif ȝow gude nocht efter wait ȝow nane ill na kin meane power toun bot gif king mak battell boun oiſt mony worthy man wallace rekkin better thay wrocht thocht beſt ȝit vther lak nocht ſernit thank scotland euer mair manheid wit quhilk thay ſchewit thair haill counſall thus demit thame amang toun seige thay thocht lang nocht ane way wyn na ſlicht counſall fand beſt thay micht sum gold tak ſen thay get na mair syne furth away thair veyage fair wallace ſaid ſelf nocht conſent bot gif toun mak v plane content tak baner ſet wall power thair realme he riddin ȝoldin quhen think thame tak ingland lang reſidence mak anſwer ſone thay ſend vnto mair thay conſentit remanent thair▪ baner tu • k vp ſet toun scotland hie honour renoun thai baner thair fra viij houri vnto none thair finance maid deliuerit gold full ſone fyue thouſand pundis gude gold ingland oiſt reſſauit vittall aboundand baith breid wyne richt glaidly furth yai gaif vther ſtuf thay lykit haif twentie dayis oiſt remanit thair bot want vittall gart thame fra fair ȝit ſtill peax oiſt ludgeit yat nicht quhill morne sone ryſſin bricht till apryll amang schawis ſchene quhen ground cled tender grene pleſand war ony 〈◊〉 herald thair durſt wallace pa quhairof king greitly aggreuit thus edward left pepill baill contrair wallace wald nocht gif battall byde feild nocht thay ſay gaif ouir caus londoun paſt way men wit queſtioun heir amang nobillis gif euer ony sa lang ingland throw force throw cace sen brutus deit vittall bot wallace greit iulius empyre hand twyis force put ingland wicht arthur al firſt weir quhen full faſt thay ſocht wallace blyith awin natiue kin come baill thay war oiſt comfort blyithar fra thair awin folk multipliand mair rochemont schyre thay fand aboundance breid aill vther purueyance oiſt wrocht erll baith quene thay went reſſauit hir fair brocht hir ane tent denner bownit al gudly thay ſeruit mony lyklie man gude purueyance quene hir brocht ane aſſay ſcho tuik gude hir thocht wallace perſauit ſaid haue na dreid nocht trow ladyis deid poyſoun men ingland wyn quene anſwerit gif poyſoun thairin ony thing quhilk brocht heir vpon ſelf firſt ſorrow ȝe ſall ſe sone efter meit ane marſchell gart abſent bot lordis thay counſall went ladyis appeirit preſence quene wallace aſkit quhat hir cūming micht mene peice ſcho ſaid haue ȝow ſocht byrnand weir baill he mony brocht ȝe grant v peice deit tre wallace anſwerit madame may nocht ingland he done ſa greit harmis v may nocht pa lichtly leif thus ȝes ſaid quene criſtin folk ar goddis ſaik ſen deſyre na mair aucht haue peice ſaid deny perfite caus ſall ſchew quhy ȝe ſeik na peice bot ȝour awin auaill quhen yat ȝour king scotland grippit haill na kin thing befoir fand wald nocht thoill richt blude land bot reft thair rent ſyne put thame ſelf deid ranſoun gold micht mak v na remeid fell fals weir ſall ſelf ſene ſoberly anſwerit quene thir wrangis amendis war maiſt fair madame ſaid aſk na mair bot wald byde v battall god iudge kennis mater haill sic thing ſcho ſaid war nocht gude think peice war beſt micht purcheſt wald ȝe grant peice trewis v tak throw ingland ſuld gar prayeris mak ȝow yame yat weir war loiſt wallace ſaid quhair ſic cūmis throw boiſt prayer force quhair ſa wrocht v helpis outher lytill nocht warly ſcho ſaid thus wyſe men he v kend ay efter weir peice finall end quhairfoir ȝe ſuld ȝour greit malice ceis end weir cheritie pei peice heuin blis leſtandnes ſall beſeik lord hie grace command peice ſen may na mair madame ſaid ȝour prayer cum thair mendis ingland think yan haue quhat ſet ȝow thus weir ſa god ȝow ſaue fra violent weir ȝe think nocht dwell madame ſaid treuth ſall ȝow tell efter dait alexanderis ring land thre ȝeir ſtuid deſolat king keipit full weill concord gude ſtait aganis richteous law ſuld haue regioun aw contrair band war haill barnage scotland ȝit neuer thirlage greit iulius tribute tuik wynning scotland bot richt ſmall ȝour fals king vnder collour mair throw band maid bruce air vndid king quhilk befoir maid throw scotland greit power yai raid bruce ſen ſyne keipit na cunnand ſaid wald nocht gang conqueis land vther men thus cace befell scotland throw demanit ſell slew eldaris greit pietie ſe preſoun ſyne lang tyme thay preſonit quhill caſſin deid thankit god ſend ſum remeid vengit preuit micht feill kin deith ſyne haue dicht rage ȝouth gart deſyre ane wyfe rewit ſair lyfe ane tratour knicht mercy gart hir de ane heſſilrig bot deſpyte rang furth trauell weir pane quhill redemit part land agane ȝour counſall deſyrit v ane trew quhilk maid scotland full graithly rew peice thay ſet ane ſubtill air xviij ſcoir deith thay hangit thair nobillis war worthy renoun coit armouris eldeſt regioun deith wethink venge micht woman al duilfully dicht mynd deith neuer ſlyde quhill god tak fra fals warld ſa wyde sutheroun ſen na pietie haif ȝour men weir neuer think ſaif bricht teiris pietie behald briſt fra ene quhen taill tald quene weipit pietie madame ȝit ȝe may nocht tempt v greit part gude left amang kyn ingland al find aneuch wyn abaiſſit ſcho mak anſwer till deir schir ſcho ſaid ſen ȝour weir peice quhat ȝow lykis beſt lat ȝour hie wit nane bot ladyis reprufe ſall nocht god ſittis abufe vpon wemen na weir begin ȝow feild na worſchip win haill pais ſelf ſall tak peice weir quhat happin mak quene grantit anſwer ſufficient sa laif plane preſent deliuerance thay held greit auaill ſtark aneuch ſchaw thair counſall wa quene hir trauell helpit nocht gold ſcho tuik yai hir brocht oiſt richt frely ſcho gaif euerie man lykit haif menſtrallis heraldis ſcho gaif aboundantle beſeikand thame hir freind thay wald quhen wallace ſaw fredome quene sadly ſaid ſuith weill he bene ſene wemen may tempt wyſeſt he bene wrocht ȝour greit gentrice ſall nocht ȝow aſſure oiſt ſall na thing quhill tyme ȝe may ſend meſſage fra ȝour king gif ſwa accord ȝour ſaik ſall better ȝour heraldis al ſall ſaifly cum ga ȝour fredome ſall trubill na scho thankit grant mony ſyſe ladyis vpon ane gudly wyſe glaidly thay drink quene gude wallace hir ladyis al lordis place hir leif ſcho tuik outtin langer baid fyue myle nicht ſouth ane nonry raid vpon morne londoun paſſit thay weſtmynſter quhair counſall lay wallace anſwer ſcho gart ſchaw king neidis nocht heir mair reheirs thing greit commend ſcho wallace gaif befoir king preſence laif trew scottis ſuld greitly appleis thocht ingliſmen thairof lytill eis • worſchip wit manheid gouernance fredome treuth key remembrance scho callit thair thair hie preſence thocht contrair thame ſtude defence sa chiftane lyke ſcho ſayis ſene ingland trow he neuer bene wald ȝe gold gif realmis rent fra honour nocht turne intent aſſouerit ȝe ar quhill ȝe may meſſage mak wyſe lordis ſum part reid ȝow tak purches peice withouttin wordis mair ingland may rew raid full ſair ȝour heraldis al pa he leif oiſt thair ſall na man thame greif thankit thay quene hir trauell king lordis war counſell hir anſwer king appleiſſit thre greit lordis thay ordanit pa thair counſall haill he fund beſt trewis tak elli thay get na reſt ane herald went haiſt may auane vaill quhair scottis lay conduct haue till thay ſaid thair counſall ſone ane conduct ſend thame till agane paſt souerance king cheiſſit thay thre lordis thing kene cliffurd wardane haill bewmont wodſtok men mekill vaill quhat thir thre wrocht ye laif ſuld ſtand yair till kingis ſelf geuin thame thair sone thay war brocht ſpeiking wallace wodſtok ſchewit furth mony ſubtill cace wallace he hard thair sophyſmis euerilk deill ȝit ſaid think mene bot weill wrang ȝe hald doi v greit outrage houſis part heritage peice plane mak thame knawin thame wyn ſen thay ar awin roxburgh berwik yat ouris lang tyme he bene handis ȝour fals king wene aſk heir al vertew band awin ȝoūg king wrang led fra scotlād ſall thame haue withouttin wordis mair deſyre lordis grantit thair richt thay haue conſentit haill na kyn thing peice thay wald nocht faill ȝoung randall londoun lord lorne band erll buchane bot tender age efter grew ane man greit vaſſalage cumyng foullis gart delyuer al quhilk efter king robert full fals wallange fled ouir durſt nocht byde yat mute picardy aſk na bute bot wald erar haue fals knicht ane thouſand fyneſt gold ſa bricht bruce aſkit bot away befoir tyme calice mony ane day king edward preuit yat yai micht nocht get legeance tuik hald scotland euer mair full glaid hait wallace reſſauit yair thay honourit richt reuerently lord scottis reioyſit concord ane hundreth hors ȝoung lordis renoū wallace come fred preſoun vnder seill king edward yan gart ſend gif ouir mak ane finall end roxburgh berwik quhilk war mekill vaill scottis men boundis haill ſyne ȝeir trewis thay promeiſt yair band wallace ſaid pa neir scotland ocht seillit thairfoir mak v boun agane beſyde northallartoun quhair king edward firſt battell hecht began thair ſall endit greit weill quene chargit meſſage hir leif veyage ane day ſet quhen thay ſuld meit thair ſeill peice withouttin proces mair vpon morne oiſt mair auyſe tranoyutit north vpon ane gudly wyſe ſet tryſt wallace thame maid inglis meſſage come mair abaid thay ſeillit peice hardely thir ar signis yat ȝe ſall tak ane bar blew ſchynand ſcheild ane bend quhyte deſyrand ay feild reid betakynis blude hardyment quhyte curage increſſand intent blew beiris criſtin man sadly anſwerit william wallace thocht criſtin na criſtin deid ga vnder loft ye lord god mot v ſpeid baith schipmaiſter steiriſman alſo baid gart thame go fyfcie men withouttin langer reſt wallace gart ray thair armour preſt aucht fourtie lufe buird laid thay law william craufurd caw ſaid thow ſum part schipman fair thow he bene vſit toun air pray tak doctrine weill luik thow ſtand ſtill ſtraitly tre quhen thay bid ſtryke ſeruice thow bane quhen warne lat doun saill agane cleland couſing cum tak ſteir hand heir waill neir ſall ſtand god gyde schip ſay na mair barge began ane ful weirlyke fair ſelf loft ane drawin ſword bad yair steiriſman lay endlang buird loud cryit ſtryke doggis ȝe ſall de craufurd leit draw saill lytill capitane lap ful ſone wald ſlynt wallace he ſone gorget hynt ouir loft keſt quhair yat ſtude quhill neis mouth ruſchit turth blude ane forgit knyfe braithly braidit weir ſchippis lappit thame barge clippit bot thay nocht feſtnit faſt craufurd drew saill ſchot thame paſt reuar cryit pieteous voce full cleir grace lyfe yat bocht v deir mercy cryit deit rude laſer mend haue ſpilt mekill blude treſpas wald mak ſum remeid mony ſaikles haue gart put deid wallace wiſt weill thocht deith war brocht fra thame chaip na wyſe micht nocht lyfe ſum reſkew micht mak ane better purpois ſyne ſone tak al rewit lyfe bene ill latine toung richt thus ſaid till neuer tuik man enemie goddis ſaik thy lyfe ȝit grant baith knyfe ſword tuik fra anone vp hand preſoner he tane vpon ſword ſcharply gart ſweir fra day furth ſuld neuer deir command thy men ſaid wallace pei thair ſchot gun
