abaid ſa yai quhen tythingis yame brocht ane hundreth wallace furth fra yame ſocht ¶the battell blak irne ſyde foreſt ca ij fyfe paſſit veſy cuntrie bot wrang warnit ingliſmen schir iohne pſewart quhē yai war paſſit fra oychell ſped haiſtely vpon wallace followit micht abirnethy tuik ludgeing firſt nicht vpon morne fyftene hundreth men blak irneſyde gydis couth ken thair wallace micht na meſſage ſend sanct iohnſtoun mak iourney kēd ingliſmen full ſubtill he bene greit wachis warnit yat nane micht pa betuene wallace ſaid mater pleſis nocht callit squyar gude guthrie biſſat al knew full weill land aſkit yame quhat deid beſt hand meſſage mak power get feill sutheroun vnbeſet wickit scottis knawis foreſt beſt thay ar caus may haue na reſt dreid far mair wallange gyde laif cūmis vpon ſyde guthrie ſaid micht get ani ouir tay sanct iohnſtoun war ganeſt way warne ramſay wald get ſuccour ſone ouir ſuith nocht weill done richt weill wait veſchell leuit nane fra wod hauin ye ferry callit arrane wallace ſaid watter awfull ſelf ſwoume trow aill na mys bot currour vſe accordis nocht leif ȝow heir ȝit leuar de throw goddis grace ſall better eſchew ſtrenth ſtrang ar men anew elchok park bot fourtie men war ſeuin hundreth gart feill sutheroun de eſchaipit weill mony vnlyklie place sa ſall heir throw help goddis grace quhill men may faſt may wod hald ſtill thy ilk man trew hardy ſa nobilly deid v fund efter na lak reid richt ouris ſuld mair ardent think freith land elli de waillit ſpeiche wit hardiment maid laif ſa cruell intent sum bad tak feild gif battell plane wallace ſaid nay thay wordis ar vane nocht leif may auantage wod v worth ane ȝei • wage win tymmer haiſt gart thame tak sillis aik ane greit barreris mak ane foir front faſt foreſt ſyde maid ane greit ſtrēth quhair yai purpoſit byde stellit thame faſt treis growand thay micht weill fra barreris pa ſe thair vaill ather ſyde syne cum agane quhen yai ſaw yair dout ſtrenth arrayit richt inglis oiſt approchit thair ſicht pſewart come yat way haue wend▪ thay war wont gydis ſa kend thair entre thay thocht haue paſſage bot ſone thay fand yat maid yame greit ſtopage ane thouſand led men armis ſtrang fyue hundreth gart iohn wallāge gang without wod nane ſuld chaip fra wallace fourtie archearis thra laif ſpeiris full nobill ane neid thair enemeis thay bikker greit ſpeid ane cruell counter barreris ſene scottis defence ſa ſicker kene sutheroun ſtude aw enter thame amang feill ground yai ouirthrew thrang ane rowme left quhair part front micht fair quha enterit agane ȝeid neuer mair fourtie thay ſlew ganewart wald haue paſt diſarayit oiſt agaſt ane part hors throw ſchot deith brocht brak ane plane sutheroun thame ſocht pſewart ſaid allace may na harme ouir greit rebute haue callit wallange aſkit counſall schiref thow art quhat may v maiſt auaill bot thay ar makis greit debait iohne wallange ſaid beſt wait ceis heirof remane heir beſyde thay may nocht lang foreſt byde falt fude thay man cuntrie war mair tyme mak thame melle thay wyn force ſtryfe feill ȝe leid ſall erar lois lyfe pſewart ſaid rede nocht tak scottis warnit reſkew ſone wil yai mak deſpite amendis think half de thairfoir number laif ane range ſelf fute fair aucht hundreth tuik lyklieſt yat yair syne bad laif byde barreris ſtill iohne wallange reull yame wallange ſaid ford wart cace ſic ane ſnair couth nocht get wallace tak ſlay promeis lyfe king edward ſall mak erll fyfe ȝone eiſt part think enter bad na mair micht ȝe barreris wyn fra thay cloſit graithly amang v ſa bot meruell thay ſall na farther ga aſſailȝe ſair quhen ȝe wit cum neir ather ſyde ſall hald thame ſteir thus pſewart thair vpon ane awfull wyſe wallace he ſene quhat he bene thair deuyſe gude men ſaid vnderſtand deid forſuith ſaid thay ar richt mekill dreid ȝone pſewart ane worthy nob • knicht ford wart weir richt hardy wyſe wicht aſſailȝe ordanis wounder ſair v harme mānis wit na mair pleſand ane wyſe chiftane ga sa chiftane lyke ſuld greit comfort awin men thay worſchip ſe ten thouſand cowartis fle sen ar ſet enemeis ilk ſyde heir force mon foreſt byde laif v abaiſſit aſſay firſt goddis ſaik cruellie craufurd left longoueill knicht fourtie thame keip barreris wicht ſextie worthy men weid meit pſewart hardy ȝeid ane maner dyke wod maid thortour ryis baldly thair abaid ane dounwith vaill sutheroun yame sone ſemblit thay ſtraikis ſair ſad scharp ſpeiris duſchand ather ſyde throw birneis bricht maid woūdis deip wyde vantage scottis thame dantit ſa na ingliſmen durſt fra fellowis ga brek array formeſt enter criſtynit blude ſe greit ſin wrangous caus he bene mony day feill ingliſmen dyke deid thair lay speiris full ſone ſplenderis ſprang ſcharp ſwordis thay hewit thrang blude briſtit throw fyne harnes maill iohne wallange al full ſcharply aſſaill vpon craufurd knicht longoueill thair power keipit barreris weill maid gude defence wit manheid micht entre feill men deith thay dicht thus atanis thay ſailȝeit ather place nane thair durſt turne fra ye barrace help wallace na man durſt pa reſkew thame ſa fell fechting ather hand thay handillit war full hait bot de na ſuccour elli thay wait wallace ſtad ſtalwart ſtour guthrie biſſat men greit valour richard wallace worthy hand pſewart meruellit yat contrair yame micht ſtād euer ſa micht byde battell place aganis thame machit face face thocht ſelf end mater weill faſt preiſſit ane gude brand ſteill dyke ane scottis man gart de wallace thairfoir hart greit pietie ane mendis haue followit faſt bot ingliſmen ſa thick betuix thame paſt vpon ane ſtraik get culd nocht vther worthy detfly deith brocht sloppis thay maid throw cheualry hardy scottis wrocht ſa worthely sutheroun ſaw thair gude men ſa dreſt langer byde yame thocht nocht beſt four ſcoir war ſlane thay wald leif ſteid fyftie al barreris deid ane trumpet blew fra wod thay draw wallange left ſicht fra ſaw ſailȝe mair thay thocht na ſpeid without wod counſall ſone thay ȝeid worthy scortis reſt thame full fane fell hurtis thay bot thame ſlane wallace bad gude comfort thankit god fairar part haue ȝone knicht pſewart he greit iourneyis bene sa fair aſſay haue bot ſeildin ſene leuar wallange wrokin ony man ȝone menȝe scottis vnto barreris ȝeid stanchit woundis couth full braithly bleid sum scottiſmen bled full mekill blude falt drink al wanting fude sum febillit faſt feill hurtis thair wallace thairfoir ſichit hart full ſair ane hat hint get watter gane vther refuge wiſt nane ane lytill ſtrand fand ran cleir watter brocht thame aboundantly drank ſelf ſyne ſaid ſober mude wyne france thocht half ſa gude day thre quarteris ouir went schir iohne pſewart he caſſin intent ſailȝe mair couth nocht preif quhill morne new men couth releif keip thame quhill thay honger ſoir cum elli de thairfoir wallange ſaid charge byde keip thame quhill cowper ryde thow ſall remane fyue hundreth thy ye morne power ſall cum till iohne wallange ſaid charge heir forſaik efter day nicht may nocht waik bot traiſtis weill thay iſche plane thocht ȝe byde al elli de pane pſewart bad byde vnderly blame command gude king edwardis name heir god avow mak beforne thay brek hyng hie morne command iohn wallange greit dreid pſewart fra thame nyne ſcoir deid nixt hand wod gude men fyfe scottꝭ blyith quhē yt yai hard ſic ſtryfe wallace drew neir tyme quhen yat ſaw wod ſyde couth wallange caw knicht he hecht ye morne hang hie cum • n v ſall thy warrand contrair king edwardis micht tak quyk ſall hang hicht ane gude lordſchip ſall gif heir eiſt ilk land thy brother he leiſit wallange wyſe full ſone couth vnderſtand lyklines wallace ſuld wyn land better war richt byde weir vpon tother ſyde ſchort auyſement wallace thay ſocht pſewart cryit ſaid beis nocht fals kynd thow art heritage edward he euill wairit greit wage heir ſall byde purpois fulfill outher de haue ſpeiche pa yai wald nocht ſpair full glaid hart wallace reſſauit yame yair rothwen ramſay renoun ane trew scot yat paſt sāct iohnſtoun thame warning maid yat pſewart followit faſt vpon wallace war thay ſair agaſt toun iſchit thair micht thre hundreth yat worthy war wicht blak irneſyde aſſemblit place wallange gane gude wallace knicht pſewart he weill thair cūming ſene ane fair plane feild cheiſit thame betuene elleuin hundreth four ſcoir scottis men war fyue hundreth ſextie thir bot ane plane feild tak wod gude wallace mak wiſt na wit thame cūmand mair hardiment fra ſtrenth pa bot quhen hard rothuen ramſay cry ouchtirhous blyith cheualry micht thay gold haue brocht ane kingis rent gude wallace micht nocht ſa weill content array thay ȝeid ather ſyde cruell ire battell bowne byde worthyer men pſewart ſemblit thair tyme edward neuer mair bot pſewart ſaw number far power ſone gart deuyde twa fecht caus knichtly thame kend iourney outher wyn end worthy scottis yat firſt amang yame baid full greit ſlauchter ingliſmen thay maid wod befoir preuit weill plane thay ſonȝeit neuer adeill curage grew thay war new begun schort reſt thay fra ryſing sone ram • ay gude worthy rothuane throw thickeſt preis gane sloppis thay maid amang ingliſmen diſſeuerit thame twentie ten quhen ſpeiris war gane ſwordis mettel • ingliſmen thair cūming ſauld full deir wallace worthynes hand feill sutheroun blude gart licht vpon ye land twa feildis togidder reillit schir iohne pſewart mony nobill man help thair lord thre hundreth ane place ſtude thair beſynes defendand mony awfull dynt quhill outwart feild tynt commounis part foreſt fled su • cour ſeik thir men ſa thame led scottis he ſene ſa mony ane rout pſewart ſtand inueronit vpon ſydis aſſailȝeit wounder ſair poleiſt plaitis poyntis peirſit bair sutheroun maid defence full cruelly occupyit nobill cheualry schir iohne ramſay wald thay ȝoldin bene wallace ſaid nay wrang ȝe mene ranſoun tak nocht begin ſic ane wyſe land ȝe may nocht win ȝone knicht auld enemie he bene sa fell v thame haue nocht ſene ſall de throw help goddis grace come pay ranſoun place sutheroun ſaw wiſt planely de reſkew nane ſuppois thay wald fle freſchly thay faucht thay enterit new vpon ſyde part worthy men thay ſlew thā pſewart ſaid allace throw wrangous thing lyfis lois deſyre king felloun knicht dou • lyfe richt nocht amang scottis full manfully wrocht biſſet ſtraik deith outtin mair wallace preuit ſword birneiſt bair pſewartis hals ettillit greit ire throw pe • ane ſtuf ſunder ſtraik ſwyre deid ground ruſchit micht wallace thus endit gude knicht remanent without mercy thay ſla gude biſſet scottis wounder wa handis ſum thay ſtikkit remeid na sutheroun paſt lyfe ſteid wod thame left feild ane range thay ſet thus micht thay get na veild ȝeid nane away contrair opinioun gude rothuen paſt agane sanct iohnſtoun schir iohne ramſay cowper caſtell raid hous tuik defence nane maid wallace craufurd yame gude guthrie richard wallace lang bene mellie longoueill lundoris baid ſtill faſtit thay lang agane thair wallange thay maid thair stewart meit drink thay fand aboundantlie power fled durſt na langer byde befoir vpon sutheroun ſyde vpon morne sanctandrois thay paſt toun biſchop bownit faſt king ingland thidder ſend rent gaif commend kingis charge durſt nocht hald ane wrangous pape yat tyran micht cald fled gat away ſee scotland wallace wald nocht ſe maid bot licht record ga • reſtoir thair richteous lord worthy knicht cowper lay gart ſpuilȝe vpon ſecund day syne ordanit men command wallace mair proces caſt doun place myndouris gart ſone peirs throw wall syne punciounis fyrit vnto gound keſt schir iohne ramſay ſyne carrell fair sutheroun fled left bot wallis bair efter pſewart thay durſt nocht tary lang scottis large throw fyfe yai rāg na ingliſmen left cuntrie bot lochleuin thair baid ane cumpanie vpon inche ſmall houſis thay licht caſtell nane bot wallit watter wicht beſyde carrell ſemblit wallace beforne purpois aſſay kingorne ane knicht muſgraif capitane ſchort auyſe purpoſit pa erar wald byde challange king wallace reckin ſic thing hous thay tuik lytill tary maid vpon morne withouttin mair abaid atouir mure quhair thay tryſt ſet neir scotland well thair ludging tuik let efter supper wallace bad thame ga reſt ſelf walk think may beſt ¶the wynning lochleuin cap iij commādit grunching yai haue done thair ſleip wallace grauhit ſone paſt lochleuin neir mydnicht auchtene warnit richt thir men weind weill come veſ • fellowis ſaid ȝow weill wit conſidder weill place vnderſtand may full greit ſkaith scotland ſouth power cum thame till thay may tak keip thair awin vpon ȝone inche richt mony men may ſyne iſche thair tyme quhen yar yai ſe byde langer heir may nocht vpon chance ȝone folk he fude traiſt weill ſufficance watter fra thame forſuith nocht fet sum vther wyle behouis v get ȝe ſall remane heir part ſtill ſelf boit ſall bring ȝow till thair weid baiſt caſtis vpon ȝone ſyde na wache man ſe held ſark tuik ſword ſa gude bund nek ſyne lap flude ouir ſwame letting nocht boit tuik men brocht arrayit weill wald na langer byde bot paſſit rowit tother ſyde inche yai tuik drawin ſwordis thay ſpairit nane thay befoir thame fand straik durris vp ſtikkit men quhair yai • ay vpon sutheroun ſadly ſembill thay threttie thay ſlew place mak defence ingliſmen na ſpace thair wemen fyue ſend ſteid wemen barnis gart neuer put deid gude thay tuik bene thair awin wallace ſaid fellowis mak ȝow knawin pur • eyante within thir wanis nocht tyne ga • ſembill v atanis lat warne ramſay gude men ilkane remane quhill ſtuf gane send furth ane man thair horſis keip drew vp boit ſyne beddis tuik ſleip wallace power neir scotland well quhilk lay befoir sone thay myſſit away sum mening maid meruellit cace ramſay bad ceis murne nocht wallace gude fra v went ſall ȝe ſe traiſt weill werrayment heid wed lochleuin paſſit ſe bot place na ingliſmen knew land bet • ix thir watteris left tythingis full ſone ȝe ſall heir eft thay war talkand wyſe meſſage come chargit thame ryſe lord ſaid denner he ȝow cald lochleuin quhilk ane lyklie hald ȝe ſall fair weill thairfoir put ſorrow thay graithit thame richt airly morrow thidder paſt wallace wit ſemblit ane full blyith fellowſchip thay lugi • yame yair quhil viij dayis end drink thay aneuch ſpend turſſit furth geir yat sutheroun brocht yair gart byrn boit sanct iohnſtoun yai fair biſchop sinklar worthy wyſe wallace come tauld auyſe thus deſyrit wallace wald ryde dunkeld soiorne wynter tyde bot ſaid nay hald nocht beſt scotland thus peice nocht reſt biſchop ſaid planely ȝe may nocht wend north men reid ȝow ſend grant quod cheiſit ane meſſingair worthy iop biſchop thair maiſter blair quhill wallace come yai baid yat gude lord yat nobill cheir yame maid wallace ſend blair preiſtis weid warne ye weſt quhair freindis greit dreid thay ſuld pa gude wallace wyn ingliſmen held thame lang twyn adam wallace lindeſay wicht rauthlic thay left went away nicht throw land lennor thay fair erll malcolme welcūmit yame full ȝair maiſter iohne blair blyith ſemblie gude grahame yair richard lūdie al robert boyd bute thame ſocht gat yai wallace na thing thay rocht bot ingliſmen betuix thame ſa ſtrang thay plane micht nocht weill gāg iop paſſit na thing wald let greit power thair couth nocht get lord cumyng erll buchaue auld inuy wald lat na man pa micht lat gude wallace • upplie erll patrik plane feild keipit ȝit pure men come preuit thair micht▪ help wallace fence scotlandis richt gude randall tender age kend part gude men murray ſend iop paſſit agane come preſence ſone befoir wallace tauld thay done bot maiſter blair ſa gude tythingis brocht cumyng wallace full lytill rocht al ingliſmen full mekill dreid fra fyfe tynt war thay trowit ſpeid duke erll tyme scotland led capitanis thay maid ingland ſyne thay ſped wallace bownit quhē thocht tyme ſuld fra sanct iohnſtoun tuik fyftie steuin ireland keirly yat wicht ingliſmen thay haldin richt waith men weid fendit thame richt welll gude wallace thay war al trew ſteill follow thay twa thocht neuer lang throw oychell thay maid yame gang mair power taryit nocht tyde keip land laif gart abyde striuiling brig wald nocht pa ſtrang power ingliſmen thair ¶the wynning erth cap iilj erth ferry thay paſſit priuatly buſkit thame ane dern ſteid thair ane cruell capitane erth dwelt ȝeir ingland borne hecht thomlin weir ane hundreth men leiding ſtill bruik land thay power ane scottis fiſchear quhilk yai tane beforne contrair gart thame ſworne thair ſeruice thay held day nicht befoir sone wallace gart iop dicht ſend furth paſſage eſpy fiſchear hapnit ſuddandly allane bot ane boy thair iop hynt ſone na dreid wald ſpair collar ane knyfe pullit goddis ſaik man aſkit mercie iop ſpeirit ſone quhat natioun art thow ane scot ſaid bot sutheroun gart vow thair ſeruice aganis full ſair bot lyfe remanit thair ſeik fiſche come north ſyde ȝe ane scot wald fane ȝow byde brocht preſence wallace scottis blyith quhen yai haue ſene yi cace boit yai micht weil paſſage haif ferry craft thocht nocht craif vpon ſyde lang ſpace thay taryit nocht ſouth land glaid hartis thay ſocht syne brak boit quhen thay war landit thair ser • ice sutheroun micht haue na mair throw mo thay paſſit full gude ſpeid torwod yat man thame thay leid wedow thair brocht tythingis wallace trew eme dwelt donypace thomlin weir preſoun ſet mair treſour ya nhe befoir micht get wallace ſaid dame ſall weill louſit morne none thairfoir ſall de scho gat thame meit quyet thay baid quhill nicht ſyne reddy ſone thay maid towart erth hall richt ſuddandly thame drew ane ſtrenth thair yat weill ye fiſchear knew draw dykis full watter wan wyſel • e thairof he warnit thame man bak ſyde led thame priuatlie fra watter wount cum ane ſmall brig gude wallace enterit hall ſelf thocht begin fra supper thay war bown ryſe ſaluſt thame vpon ane awfull wyſe men followit ſuddandly atanis haiſtie ſorrow raſit thay wanis ſcheirād ſwordis ſcharply yame dang feill flure fellit thame amang thomlin weir wallace ſelf he met ane felloun ſtraik ſadly vpon ſet throw heid ſwyre throw ye coiſt claif worthy scottis faſt ſtikkit laif keipit durris deith thame dicht chaip away sutheroun na micht sum wyndois ſocht haue brokin bot nocht full fey maid rout fyre buſchit blude ſa reid ane hundreth men ſlane ſteid wallace ſocht quhair vncle ſuld ane deip coif ſet dulefullie quhair watter ſtude irnis ſtrang wallace full ſone brais vp dang myrk hoill brocht ſtrenth liſt bot noyis hard na thing elli wiſt sa blyith befoir warld nocht bene thair ſichit quhen wallace ſene dykis deid bodyis thay keſt graithit place thame lykit beſt maid full gude cheir wyſe wachis thay ſet quhill neir day thay ſleip withouttin let quhen thay ſicht ſpuilȝeit place hy fand ganand geir baith gold iowalry ouir day quyet held thame ſtill quhē sutheroun come reſſauit yame gude yat laubour ye scottis ful bane ingliſmen come bot nane ȝeid agane wemen barnis put preſoun caif sa thay micht mak na warning laif steuin ireland keirly yat wicht keipit port vpon ſecund nicht befoir day worthy scottis rais turſſit gude geir torwod gais remanit thair quhill nicht cūmin hand syne bownit thame quyet throw land wedow ſone fra thay war paſſit dout ane ſeruand ſend leit wemen pa fra erth quhair yat yame lykit beſt ſpeik thame went weſt ¶how wallace brynt ingliſmen dunbertane cap v vallace ſelf ſicker gyde nicht dunbartane way cheiſit richt day nicht lang vnto toun full priuatly thay gang mekill ingliſmen occupyit gude waallce ſone throw ane dark garth hyit vnto ane hous quhair wont ken ane wedow dwelt freind cheualry caſtell thay weind pa let worthy scottis ſa hardly thame ſet fourtie atanis derfly ground thay bair remanent effrayit war ſa ſair langer feild thay na micht byde bot feirſly fled fra thame ather ſyde scottis thair weill he ye entre win ſlew thair hous fundin syne flearis followit wounder faſt na ingliſman lyfe thair fra thame paſt wemen ſone thay ſeiſit hand keipit thame clois warning wald cum pei aganis sutheroun thair malice ceis trew scottis ordanit waryſoun quha taltit grantit remiſſioun dumfreis wald na langer byde sutheroun fled • f scotland ilk ſyde ſey land without langer abaid caſtellis tounꝭ yan wallace chiftanis maid reullit land put gude reſt trew keiperis quhilkis traiſtit beſt gude dowglas ȝow tald air keiper fra drumlanerik air becaus sutheroun ſie thing wrocht wyfe wraith bot yat ſcho ſchew nocht vnder couert hir malice held perfyte ane serpent waitis hir tyme yat ſcho may byte dowglas oft ſcho wrocht full mekill cair leif quhill farther mair bot sutheroun men durſt yan na caſtellis hald thay left scotland befoir ȝow tald saif ane mortoun ane capitane feirs ſell held dundie wallace wald nocht dwell thidder paſt lappit quhen mortoun ſaw yat dout aſkit leif thair lyfis ga wallace denyis ſayis beis nocht ſwa laſt capitane ingland yat heir gaif leif haill men pa thow ſall forthink ſic maiſtrie mak ingland ſall exempill tak sic men weind fra thyne haue worne thow ſalbe hangit ſuppois thy king ſworne▪ gart command na scottis ſuld yame ſpeik confermit ſeige ſaid ſall v wreik ingliſmen ſkill dundie skrymgeour maid thair conſtabill ane ballingair ingland thair paſt tay come quhitbie fair londoun ſend tald cace hyng mortoun ſa vowit wallace befoir tyme edward power ȝeid weir france na dreid befoir trowit scotland win quhen thay warnit men sūmoundis yai maid chargit bruce name vther leuit vnder crown biſchop barroun cum summoun quhē wallace twyis throw grace fred scotland tyran king tuik planely vpon hand ſic deſyre micht haue na reſt wyn trowit weir thay wald na mair begyn leif king makand ordinance purpois ſpeik ſum thing france ingliſmen guyan held weir frenche folk yai full mekill deir king counſall ſone thair wittis keſt get wallace thame thocht beſt guyan land ingliſmen thay ſchuip thay thus haiſt thay may thay traiſtit gif scotland war weill ſtad wallace wald cum thame promeiſt ſamyn herald befoir scotland thay commandit ordanit ſuld pa scotland without langer delay sluce al gudly may reddy schip paſt cais tayis mouth baid hauin tai quhair wallace ye ſailȝe ſtill reſſauit herald gude thair writ red ſaid thame wyſe ane anſwer ſone couth thame nocht deuyſe honeſt iunis herald ſend wallace coiſt richt baldly ſpend quhill tyme ſaw vther materis ȝeid anſwer ſuld haue withouttin dreid wit france thocht wallace commend scotland herald thay ſend praiſe deid al deſcriptioun tane thair men diſcretioun clerkis knichtis heraldis ſaw bot heirof nocht reheirs aw wallace ſtature greitnes hicht iudgit thus diſcretioun ſicht ſaw baith cheuall weid nyne quarteris large hicht deid thrid part lenth ſchulderis braid richt ſemely ſtrang richt luſtie ſe lymmis greit ſtalwart pais ſound braunis hard armis lang round handis maid richt lyke ane palmeir manlyke mak naillis lang cleir proportionat fair lang viſage richt ſad ſpeiche abill curage braid breiſtit heich ſturdy craig greit lippi round neis ſquair treit broundant broun hair browis breis licht cleir aſper ene lyke dyamantis bricht vnder chyn left ſyde ſene hurt ane wen cullour ſanguene woundis mony diuers place bot fair haill weill keipit face rich al keipit na propir thing gaif yat wan lyke alexander king tyme pei meik ane mayd ſuld quhair weir approchit richt hector scottis men richt gude credence gaif bot knawin enemyis yai couth nocht diſſaif thir properteis war iudgit france ane gudly remembrance maiſter iohn blair patroun couth reſſai • wallace buik breuit laif bot heirof tuik lytill heid lauborous mynd vther deid dundie seige twa thouſand chargit thy nane ſuld chaip lyfe ſteid sutheroun war bot put yame deid skry • geour grantit richt faithfully byde aucht thouſand wallace fra ryde sanct iohnſtoun thre dayis graithit yair ſad auyſe towart ſouth fair king edward tyme ordanit ten thouſand haill pa full glaid ȝoung wodſtok ane lord mekill micht • striuiling brig ordanit thame full richt thair byde entrie weir wallace men fechtand ſtill meit thay carllis come egir firſt leit draw wallace syith deliuer heich ouirlap ſwyith ane akwart ſtraik hit churll heid derfly ground he left deid tother met ouir lap syith ſa kene firſt thair power • laik wallace followis ſone fyft ouirtais straik deith na farther gais syne ſped ſone vnto men agane thay knichtis brother ſlane fyftie ſex derfly deith dicht except ſeuin men fled thair ſicht fyue mawaris al wallace ſelf met frenchemen ſen ſyne na ſic tryſt ſet becaus thay brocht ſic ane cace king hard tell weill chaipit wallace send ſone ſyne prayit houſhald leif gude ſaiftie thrawart conditiounis richt greit deſpite thay ſpak ay scotland quhill ane day hapnit vpon hand wallace thay war leuit thame allane auenture ane hous ſtane thay vſit beir na wappinis hall thay trowit thairfoir ane mys yai micht fall thair commonnit thay scotland ſcornefully wallace ſaid ȝe wrang v vtterly sen ar bund freindſchip ȝour king v pleſit thing scottiſmen he helpit realme fra dreid think face tene gude hand quhill neis mouth ene throw braith blaw buſchit blude grouflingis groūd ſmoit quhair ſtude tother hynt wallace ſteid weill weind fellow bene deid agane greif grippit ſair quhill lang tyme france wald haif lattin yame traiſt weill treuth thus war thay gane deid thocht frenche mē lykis yairof reid al ceis put ryme better quha richt luik tyme mony greit lord diſpleiſit france bot ye gude king yat knew haill chance richt greit deſpite scotland ſpokin thay paſſit ouir quhill yat vpon ane day nane thame yat durſt vndertak done wrang yairfoir battell mak ¶how wallace ſlew lyoun barrace cap iij royall roy ane hie worſchip gaif conquerour honourit ouir ye laif ane fell lyoun yi king gart brocht within barrace greit harme yat wrocht tyrliſit irne na mair power gaif wodnes exceidit laif bot fair richt felloun deid ſtrang ſtrenth gart men feid keipit clos men beſtiall court yair dwelt twa squyarꝭ greit vaill couſingis war ye cāpioūis twa quhilk befoir wallace hapnit ſla ane band thay maid preuy concluſioun thair power wirk confuſioun ony meane throw fraud ſubteltie efter yairfoir yai thocht nocht de deith ſchame ſa yat yai micht bring vpon ane tyme thay went vnto king scot thay ſaid ȝe ſa weill fair mak ſeis nocht heir bot wald vndertak greit force put confuſioun deſyris fecht ȝour lyoun bad v aſk ȝow battell ſtrang ȝe grant leif barrace gang sadly agane thame anſwerit king sair forthinkis deſyris ſic thing bot nouther greif ȝit pleſa • ce deny wallace quhat deſyris france went thay furth ſone met wallace ane figurat taill thay tauld yat cace wallace thay ſaid king deſyris ȝe direnȝe battell ſa cruell ſe chargis ȝow fecht lyoun wallace anſwerit haiſtie concluſioun ſall quhat kingis power richt glaidly fulfill paſſit vnto king mair ane lord court quhen approchit thair vnwyſelie ſpeirit without prouiſioun wallace dar ȝe ga fecht lyoun ſaid ȝe ſa king ſuffer ȝour ſelf gif ȝe ocht better quhat ȝe mair thing admittit wallace ſuld vnto lyoun pa king chargit bring gude harnes ſaid nay god ſcheild fra ſic cais ſuld tak gif faucht ane man bot ane dog nocht armis haue nane bot ſinglil ga ane greit mantill hand ta ane gude ſword tuik na mair abandoundly barrace enterit thair greit cheinȝeis wrocht ye ȝet gin pullit quhen wallace thairin wod lyoun wallace quhair ſtude rampand brayit deſyrit blude round pollis mantill rocht ſa akwart bak ȝit wallace ta gude ſword birneiſt ſteill body twa cuttit euerilk deill syne king raikit greit ire ſaid loud ȝour deſire wair ane scot lichtly vane thair doggis yat ȝe ȝit wald haue ſlane ga bring yame furth ſen man doggis quell bidding quhill yat ȝow dwell ganis full weill graith scotland greiter deidis yair men he tane hand ane dog battell encheif ȝow france euer tak leif king perſauit yat wallace greuit sa erniſtly aſkit leif pa rewit mynd hapnit ſa sa lewd ane deid lat vnderta knawand worſchip ye greit nobilnes quhilk ſprang yat tyme mony place hamely ſaid ſuld diſpleis ȝow nocht ȝe deſyrit bred neuer thocht faith aw crown france thocht neuer charge ȝow ſic chance bot men vaill aſkit ȝow wallace anſwerit god mak ane vow lykit neuer ſic battell vpon ane dog na worſchip win king conſauit falſet wrocht squyaris baith preſence brocht culd nocht deny quhen thay come befoir thair treſpas thay tald withouttin moir king commandit yai ſuld done deid smoit thair heidis without • ny remeid campiounis lo inuy cauſ • e ſuddād deith wallace yame brocht throw cais squyaris al fra yair falſnes kend inuy yame brocht baith ane ſuddand end lordis behald inuy euill dragoun cruell fyre byrnis regioun nocht yat aboundis inuy ſum miſcheif bringis thame haiſtely forſaik inuy thow ſall better ſpeid heirof na farther reid bot mater befoir began ſall declair al planely qvhen wallace ſaw thay inuy langer byde couth nocht yan planely better thocht scotland auenture tak outher leif de help awin far mair pleſance thair byde welth france haill mynd manheid curage planely ſet wyn bondage scotland agane fra pane mekill ſchoir vowit ſuld elli de thairfoir king he ſene gude wallace ſet letter gaif withouttin let quhilk lait fra scotland ſend wallace ſaw weill yair harmis kend firſt writ thairto accordiall thame ſupple thocht wald nocht faill quhairof ſuld heirof lang proces mak wallace france ane gudly leif tak king he ſene wald nocht elli chalmer went behald micht nocht greit langour quhen wallace remufe king keipit kyndnes ay lufe iowellis gold worſchip ſaif bad thame gif al mekill wald haif lordis ladyis weipit wounder faſt quhen wallace thair ſa tuik leif paſt na man schip couert ſaill away sa ſicht thay war day elchok dwelt ane wallace couſing deir craufurd hecht ye hous quhē yai come neir bak ſyde wallace ane wyndo fand callit ſyne craufurd come hand fra tyme wiſt gude wallace barn ordanit yame ane place ane mow corne biggit thame cloſit weill nane micht perſaif thair bot ane place quhair meit yame brocht bedding al gudly mocht ane dern hoill furth north ſyde thay vnto watter quhair wallace glaid four dayis fyue reſt yai ſoiornit thair quhill meit gane craufurd bownit mair sāct iohnſtoun yair purueyance ingliſmen thocht tuik mair aboundantly wount ony tyme befoir thay haue tane put preſoun • oir quhat gaiſtis tell thay maid requeiſt ſaid bot ane kirking feiſt ȝit thay preſumit cūming wallace knawledge get yai ſet ane ſubtell race thay leit pa thing bocht syne efter ſone haiſt thay mocht harnes ȝeid power toun aucht hūdreth men wt buttellar maid yame boun followit dreich quhill yat yi man come hame wallace ſaw ſaid ſeruit blame ſleiping ane fell viſioun tald till ingliſmen thow ſuld haue ſald craufurd ſaid bene torment ſair ingliſmen diſpair thairfoir ryſe vp ſone ſum ſuccour ſe dreid full ſair thay ſet wachis worthy ſcottis yai land nocht richt bot elchok park neir heir beſyde firſt ſail ȝe think thair abyde nyntene thay war craufurd gude wil twentie man number fulfill park thay tuik wallace ane place he ſene ot greit holing yat grew baith heich grene thortour treis ane maner ſtrenth maid war wyn thay thocht gar feill de wod thick bot lytill breid lenth yai meit yai thocht hald ſtrenth ingliſmen paſt craufurdis place fand barn ludgeing wallace craufurdis wyfe handis thay haue tane aſkit hir quhat way scottis gane richt weill thay trowit wallace ſuld yair fra france tay cūmit throw ſe scho wald nocht tell boiſt ȝit rewaird thā buttellar ſaid ouir lāg thow he bene ſpaird thair grew matalent ire gart thame big ane braid byrnand fire sutheroun ſwore yairin ſcho ſuld brynt wallace ſaid ſcho ſall nocht end greit ſin war ȝone faikles wicht ſla ſcho ſuld end faith yair ſall de left ſtrenth plane feild ta loud cryit ſaid lo heir thy fa thinkis thow ſchame tormēt ane wyfe cum firſt mak end ſtryfe fra buttellar feild gude wallace ſene auld malice woxe neir wod tene vpon ye scottis thay ſchuip greit mane gude wallace ſone ſtrenth tuik agane ane feill bikker ingliſmen began aſſailȝeit ſair mony cruell man bot yai within war nobill defence maid greit debait force violence entrie fyftene thay put deid laif remouit fra ſteid ȝe • array agane ſailȝe new wallace beheld quhilk weill weir knew fellowis ſaid agane place thay nocht faill bot thus ſtandis cace ȝone knicht thinkis deuyde men seir placis ſuith ȝe ſall weill ken agane v preif may v behouis ſum vther way ſe contrair thair micht ane gude defence mak better thy gentrice thow wald th • ȝeild wallace ſaid thy vnſkilfull thow wald quhilk ouir hi • ane mi ȝoldin better prufe quhome aſkit greit god abu • e euerilk day ſen wit man befoir werk ȝeild nocht heir quhill nyne houri day buttellar ſend furth ye chak wache ilk ſyde ilk place baldly bownit byde thus ſtill thay baid quhill day began peir ane thick myſt fell ye planeit nocht cleir wallace aſſayit place leit wald ony ane place brek quhill buttellaris men away fra couth ga help laif quhen yai ſaw ſa wallace faſt ſped thame ſteid quhair buttellar baid feill men yai draif deid worthy quhen thay come neir ane nobill knicht quhilk name hecht hew dundas ſchir iohn scot ane wyſe worthy knicht stra • herne ane man mekill micht thair greit part heritage dundas siſter mariage paſſand thay war micht na langer leſt ingliſmen thair fewtie feſt lord breichen ſic cūnand yame maid king edward hald thair landis braid bot fra thay ſaw wicht wallace held vp thair handis thankit god grace greit help quhilk ſend yame yair methuen wod ane aſſent thay fair sone gat thame meit beſtiall thay fand reſtit day quhē nicht cūmin hand birnane wod reſting ar thay gane quhair yai haue fund ye wyld tame countrie maid bair bot ſtrenthis thair fude leuit nane thir worthy ſcottis yan maid ane pieteous mane schir iohne scot ſaid far rather de gude name leif airis fre byde bund ſubiectioun quhen wallace ſaw thir gude men renoun hunger ſtad almaiſt micht leif na mair wit ȝe thame ſichit wounder ſair gude men ſaid caus ȝour deſyre ſall amend mi leif ȝow fre ſum cheuiſance allane bownit ga prayit thame byde quhill micht cum agane ouir ane hill paſſit plane ovt thair ſicht ane foreſt ſyde ſet doun vnder ane aik byde bow sword lenit ane tre anguiſche greif grouf ſa turnit pieteous mane man ſaid thus war ane hie renoun micht quick leid sanct iohnſtoū lo lyis may grippis waill wappinis ſall haue nane auaill ſall bynd contrair leid thus bak ſyde ȝone hill sa men ſall na thing knaw tother four aſſentit ſaw thir fyue maid thame vnto wallace thocht throw force bynd place quhat trowit thir fyue hald wallace doun manlyeſt man ſtarkeſt perſoun leuand al ſtude ſic richt traiſt weill god deidis he ſicht thay grippit ſleip braid quhat menis ſadly wallace ſaid turnit vp armis thrang thay tratouris knichtly feir dang ſtarkeſt man hand hynt harnis dang ane tre ſword gat ſone efter rais campioun lyke amang four gais euer ane man gart de ane dynt quhē twa deid ye tother thre wald ſtynt maid thame fle bot na bute nane leuand micht fra pa fute followit faſt ſone deith thame brocht chyld ſadly agane ſocht quhat thow heir ye chyld ane pail face kneis fell aſkit wallace grace thame knew na thing yair thocht ſeruice thay bad wrocht quhat beiris thow thair bot meit ye chyld ſay ga hounger ſa ſleipand wappinles sa weill recouerit wallace cais planely force vincuſt enemeis fyue men wit queſtioun diſcryue withouttin glois tell furth taill come meit fellowſchip aſkit haill thair deſyre wallace na anſwer ȝald quhair fyue deid led yame furth tald greitly diſpleiſit cheualry ane chiftane thay held fantaſy walk allane wallace ſobir mude sayis heirof cum na thing bot gude law land agane full faſt thay ſocht speirit yi chyld gif couth wi yame ocht quhair thay micht beſt purueyance win nane ſaid countrie within al far knaw quhill yat ȝe cum doun rannoch haw lord he ſtuf baith aill breid vernage king edward takis full mekill wage wallace ſaid ſelf ſall ȝour gyde knaw ſteid ather ſyde throw wyld la • gydit thame full richt rannoch hall brocht thame yat ſame nicht ane wache full ſone thay ta ane scot ȝit wald nocht ſla bot gart tell maner place thus enterit thay within ane lytill ſpace ȝet thay wan caſtell yair nane bot mud wall wicht withouttin lyme ſtane wallace haiſt ſtraik vp chalmer dure richt fuit ſtalwart ſture thay within walknit ſuddandly lord gat vp mercy cry fra tyme wiſt gude wallace thair thankit god ſyne ſaid thir wordis mair trew man wyn aganis ingliſmen ſuppois lykit ill scottis ar yat hous ȝour command baldly ſall bow natioun gude wallace pietie tuik aithis thame ſyne meit aſkit gude cheir yai maid quhill licht day ye morne trew man ſone ſemblit beforne thre sonis yat ſtalwart war bald twentie men kyn houſhald wallace blyith thay maid ſic ſupplie said thank god yat thus multiplie day ouir gude lyking thay reſt wachis thay waill keip weſtland men arrane rauchlie fra thay warnit thay cum thus purpois tuik north yai ryde na ingliſman durſt thair gait abyde quhome wallace tuik yai knew ye auld ranſoun fra come hame fle thay mak yame boun scottiſmen ſemblit wallace faſt awfull feir throw land thay paſt strenthis left wit ȝe deſolait agane thir folk na man durſt mak debait rayit battell thay raid abirdene haill number vij thouſand ſene bot ingliſmen left toun waiſt euerilk ſyde away thame haiſt land left nouther mair le lord bewmont tuik ſey buchane ne throw scotland manifeſt plane lordis fled hart wounder fane knicht clement ro come ſuddandly murray land thair gude cheualry hous narne yat guid knicht weil he tane slew capitane gude men mony ane murray buchane land come thay ſeik bewmont bot paſt away thir gude men wallace paſſit richt quhē wallace ſaw ſchir iohne ramſay ye knicht vther gude men bene fra lang greit curage yan raiſit thame amang land reullit lykit beſt sanct iohnſtoun ſyne raid yai wald reſt ¶the seige sanct iohnſtoun euerilk port ane ſtalwart wache maid confermit ane seige ſteidfaſtly abaid biſchop sinklair gude haiſt dicht come bute ſemely men ſicht ilis rauchlie arrane lindeſay boyd gude men mony ane adam wallace barroun ricardtoun full ſadly ſocht wallace renoun sanct iohnſtoun baid sailȝe ſtill sutheroun men yai micht weill pa thair way thair durſt na enemie bot fled away land al ſe toun wrocht wallace martyrit ye ſuith ȝow tell wer oſwald edmond edward panis tell men armis led ane full greit rout ane bald ſpreit wallace blent ane preiſt aſkit deit tre king edward commandit clergie ſaid charge pane lois lyfe nane ſa bold ȝone tyran ſchryfe he rung lang incontrair hienes ane bliſſit biſchop ſone preſent place canterbery richteous lord aganis king maid richt record ſaid ſelf ſall heir confeſſioun gif haue micht incontrair thy crown thow throw force ſall ſtop fra thing vow god quhilk richteous king ingland ſall interdyte mak knawin thow art ane heretyke sacrament kirk ſall geif syne tak thy chois ſterf lat leif war mair vaill worſchip thy crown keip ſic ane lyfe thy bandoun land gude yat thow he • bot couetiſe ye ay fra honour dre • thow he thy lyfe rung wrangous deid ſall ſene thy ſeid king gaif charge thay ſuld biſchop ta bot wyſe lordis counſallit lat ga wyſe men ſaid yat deſyre richt wallace raikit thair ſicht ſadly hard confeſſioun end humbly god ſpreit commend lawly ſeruit hartly deuotioun vpon kneis ſaid ane oriſoun leif tuik weſtmynſter raid cleuch men yai buir wallace baid vnto ane place martyrdome tak deith na furthering mak fra firſt nicht tane scotland thay keipit ſamin band na thing he done gude bot ingliſmen ſeruit cairfull fude warldly lyfe deſyris ſuſtenance thocht gat incontrair pleſance thay threttie dayis bandis yai durſt flaik quhill bund ane scamyll aik irne cheinȝeis war baith ſtark kene ane clerk thay ſet heir quhat wald mene thow scot ſaid yat ſa greit wrang he done thy fatall hour thow ſeis approchis ſone thow ſuld mynd remember thy myſdeid clerkis may quhen yai yair pſalmes reid criſtin ſaullis yat makis thame pray thair number yow may ane thay thow ſeis force thow man deceis wallace ſaid thy round reheirs thow he na charge ſuppois done mys ȝone bliſſit biſchop he hecht ſall haue blys trow weill god ſall admit thy ſimulate wordis ſall conſcience ſmit comfort haue way ſuld gang maiſt pane feill byde heir ſa lang ſaid clerk king oft ſend till thow micht haue scotland thy hald ceiſſit thy ſtryfe sa ane lord rungin furth thy lyfe wallace ſaid thow ſpeikis michty thing leſtit gottin richteous king fra worthy bruce reſſauit crown thocht haif maid ingland bandoun vtterly ſuld haue bene quhat pleiſit ſaif thy king ſpill weill ſaid clerk ſe thow repentis nocht wickitnes thow he ane felloun thocht nane warld he ſa mony • lane thairfoir aſk think thow ſuld bane grace king ſyne barnage wallace ſmylit ane lytill langage grant ſaid ſum ingliſmen ſlew querrell thocht nocht half anew muifit na weir bot wyn awin baith god mā ye richt full weill he knawin thy fruſtrat wordis doi nocht bot tyris command goddis name lat ane schiref gart clerk ſone fra pa richt thay durſt grantit quhat wald ane pſalter buik wallace euer fra chyldheid wald nocht ſeuer better trowit veyage ſpeid bot diſpuilȝeit weid grace aſkit lord cliffurd knicht lat haue pſalter buik ſicht gart ane preiſt oppin befoir hald quhill thay done quhat yat yai wald steidfaſt red ocht thay thair feill sutheroun ſaid wallace feld na ſair gude deuotioun ſa beginning continewit yair ſwa ending quhill ſpeiche spreit atanis fair leſtand blys trow euer mair nocht tell deuydit fyue partis ordanit pa ȝit ſpreit thus lyklines weill wallace lyfe quha he ane better • eill may ſchew furth mair writ eloquence he done diligence efter proſe geuin fra latine buik quhilk maiſter blair tyme vnder tuik fair latine compylit ane end gude witnes mair commend biſchop sinklair lord dunkell gat buik confirmit ſell verray treuth thairof na dreid ſelf hard greit part wallace deid purpois haue ſend rome father kirk yairin gif dome bot maiſter blair al ſchir thomas gray efter wallace thay leuit mony ane day thir twa knew beſt gude ſchir williamis deid fra ſextene ȝeir quhill nyne twentie ȝeid fourtie fyue wallace age cald tyme yat sutheroun ſald thocht mater nocht pleſance ſuithfaſt deid worthy auance worthy men reidis rurall dyte blame nocht buik thocht imperfyte ſuld haue thank ſen na trauell ſpaird trauell na man hecht rewaird na charge king vther lord greit harme thocht gude deid ſuld ſmord haue ſaid heir neir proces gais fenȝeit nocht freindis ȝit fais coiſtis heirof na man bund ſentence na le bot al mekill reheirſit nocht sa worthely nobill wallace wrocht bot ane point grant ſaid ane mi thir twa knichtis ſuld blamit knicht wallace cragy richteous lord lyddaill al gart mak wrang record allartoun mure ye crown tuik ane day get battell myne author ſay thir twa gart ſay ane vther wyſe maiſter blair part ſuppryſe go nobill buik fulfillit ſentence suppois thow barrane eloquence go worthy buik fulfillit worthy deid bot help langage thow he neid quhen gude makeris rang weill scotland greit harme nane thame fand ȝit thair part weill auance byde tyme remembrance ȝow beſeik ȝour beneuolence quha nocht loif lak nocht eloquence weill knawin ane rurall man heir he done al gudely toung neuer ornate termis embrace beſeik god geuar grace maid hell eird ſet ye heuin abufe till v grant deir leſtand lufe ¶thus endit williame wallace wicht behind left nocht ſic ane knicht worthynes deid hand fra thraldome thryis fred land ¶imprentit
